## EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK (PATH A)

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-12)** — **governance and editorial-boundary decision only.** **PATH A:** **REDUCED-SCOPE PAGES CMS EDITORIAL MODEL.**

**Builds on:** **POST-MIGRATION LEGACY SYSTEM AUDIT — LOCK** and **PAGES CMS VALIDATION AUDIT — LOCK** — **does not** supersede their inventories or safety findings; **adds** the **formal product stance** for what **Pages CMS** is allowed to **mean** in this repository.

### Decision (locked)

**Pages CMS** is **officially** treated as:

- a **constrained** editorial surface  
- intended for **safe scoped** content editing (**Zierota-facing** profile in **`.pages.yml`**)  
- **not** a full canon-administration environment  
- **not** a full **Decap** parity target  

**Full admin / canon authority** remains **outside** the Pages CMS surface (**Decap** + **Identity** + direct **Git** workflows and any **future Git-first governance** processes).

---

### 1. Pages CMS role (authoritative)

| Aspect | Definition |
| ------ | ---------- |
| **Audience / posture** | **Zierota-facing** editorial surface — **low-risk** layer for approved **limited** field work. |
| **Safety model** | **Constrained** editing — governance-hardened **readonly** on sensitive keys; editable **`title`**, **`meaning`**, **`facets`**, **`terms`** per current **`.pages.yml`** (as **documented** in **PAGES CMS VALIDATION** §1 — **this lock does not change** that file). |
| **Workflow** | **GitHub-authenticated** commits to the working branch (typically **`pages-cms-prototype`** for Cloudflare). |
| **Authority level** | **Operational** convenience for **scoped** text/list adjustments — **not** ownership of canon law, schema, or archive lifecycle. |

---

### 2. Non-goals (explicit)

**Pages CMS** is **not** intended for:

- **full** canon governance or **doctrine authority** (deep **`doctrine`** / dossier restructuring via CMS)  
- **unrestricted** sigil creation / deletion / row lifecycle (**`create`/`delete`** on file entry are **false** today; **new slug** workflows are **out of band**)  
- **unrestricted** structural editing of the codex pack (reordering governance, bulk field refactors)  
- **archive** authority (deprecation / archival reason fields **readonly** on Zierota profile)  
- **schema** authority (**`sigils.schema.json`**, validator rules, field additions)  
- **migration** authority (branch moves, data mass transforms)  
- **deployment** authority (Cloudflare / Netlify project settings, production branch switches)  
- **infrastructure retirement** (removing Decap, Identity, redirects, **`netlify.toml`**)  

---

### 3. High-authority operations (outside Pages CMS)

The following **remain outside** the **Pages CMS** boundary — to be done via **git PR**, **Decap** (where still appropriate), **dedicated locks**, or **future Git-based governance** — **not** by widening Pages without a **new lock**:

- **Canon maturation** (full dossier passes, **`underlay`**, deep **`doctrine`** edits when policy says **git/Decap**)  
- **Archive / deprecation governance** (**`status`**, **`visibility`**, **`deprecatedReason`**, **`archivedReason`**, etc.)  
- **Schema evolution** and **validator** changes  
- **System governance** (routes, components, discoverability rules)  
- **Structural codex operations** (new public sigil **ingestion pipeline**, **`slug`** / identity keys)  
- **Advanced doctrine editing** beyond the **narrow** Pages-allowed set  
- **Infrastructure retirement** and **deployment governance**  

---

### 4. Decap / Netlify Identity status (clarified)

- **Preserved temporarily** — **no** retirement phase **started**; **no** admin **replacement** **completed**.  
- **Primarily treated as:** **legacy fallback**; **rollback / admin continuity** path; **higher-authority editorial surface** relative to **PATH A** Pages scope.  
- **Retirement** is **deferred** — **no** retirement **execution** is authorized by this lock or by **POST-MIGRATION** / **PAGES CMS VALIDATION** alone.  

---

### 5. Future strategy (preferred direction — planning only)

- **Pages CMS** **continues** as the **intentionally limited** Zierota editorial interface.  
- **Advanced / admin** workflows **gradually** move toward **Git-based** governance (PR review, documented ingestion, explicit locks) — **not** toward **silent** Pages config expansion.  
- **Eventual Decap retirement** is **possible only after**: a **rollback** window and **admin / editor population** strategy are **resolved**, and a **dedicated execution lock** authorizes cleanup.  

---

### 6. Operational role classification (extended — PATH A)

| Role | Meaning in this project |
| ---- | ------------------------ |
| **Canonical production** | **Cloudflare Pages** + **`pages-cms-prototype`** + **`dist`** from **`npm run build`**. |
| **Constrained editorial surface** | **Pages CMS** / **`.pages.yml`** (**Zierota** profile) — **PATH A**. |
| **Fallback admin surface** | **Decap `/admin`** + **Identity** + **Git Gateway** — continuity when Pages/GitHub path is insufficient. |
| **Legacy preserved** | **Netlify** path, **redirect** scripts, **`public/admin/*`**, **`netlify.toml`** — intact until **execution lock**. |
| **Future retirement candidate** | Same systems as **POST-MIGRATION** §7 — **not** active; **governance-deferred**. |
| **Governance authority boundary** | **High-impact** decisions and **canon integrity** gates live **outside** Pages — see §§ **2–3** above. |

---

### 7. Governance rules (PATH A — binding)

- The **constrained editorial surface** must **remain intentionally limited**.  
- **Avoid accidental privilege expansion** — **no** drive-by **`.pages.yml`** widening without a **dedicated governance lock**.  
- **No hidden parity creep** toward **unrestricted** admin through incremental UI convenience.  
- **Future expansions** of Pages scope require a **dedicated governance lock** (masters + explicit scope).  
- **Editorial convenience must not override canon integrity** — **`npm run build`** / **`validate:content`** / **ingestion pipeline** rules remain **authoritative**.  

---

### 8. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** repository configs were **changed** for this lock (**`.pages.yml`**, **`public/admin/config.yml`**, **`netlify.toml`**, **`package.json`**, etc.).  
- **No** editorial **permissions** or **Identity** integration were **altered** by this documentation.  
- **No** systems were **removed** or **disabled**.  
- **No** migrations were **executed**.  
- **Governance decision only** — **operational reality** preserved: **Cloudflare Pages** canonical production; **`pages-cms-prototype`** canonical branch; **Pages CMS** **viable** for **scoped** editing; **Decap/Identity** **preserved**.  

---

## ZIEROTA ADMIN ACCESS — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-12)** — **documentation + implementation audit only.** **Does not** delete **Decap**, **Netlify Identity**, **`public/admin/*`**, **`netlify.toml`**, **`public/_redirect-identity.js`**, or **legacy** redirect behavior; **does not** change **schema**, **`sigils.json`**, **visibility** rules, **admin UI** design, or **blindly** migrate CMS systems. **Builds on** **EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK** (**PATH A**), **PAGES CMS VALIDATION AUDIT — LOCK**, **POST-MIGRATION LEGACY SYSTEM AUDIT — LOCK**, **ZIEROTA ONLINE ADMIN SETUP** locks, and **CLOUDFLARE PAGES MIGRATION — VALIDATED**.

**Purpose:** State the **safest current** admin **login** posture for **Zierota** under **Cloudflare Pages** + **Pages CMS** + **PATH A**, while **keeping** **Decap** + **Identity** as **authorized** fallback and **higher-authority** editorial.

---

### 1. Admin login paths that exist today (repo-inspected)

| Path | What it is | Auth / backend | Notes from repo |
| ---- | ---------- | -------------- | ----------------- |
| **A. Pages CMS (PATH A)** | **`.pages.yml`** at repo root; **Cloudflare Pages** production branch **`pages-cms-prototype`** carries the file | **GitHub** (user or GitHub App per Pages CMS product); **direct git** commits — **no** Netlify Identity | **Constrained** profile: **`title`**, **`meaning`**, **`facets`**, **`terms`** editable; canon/governance fields **readonly** (**PAGES CMS VALIDATION AUDIT — LOCK**). |
| **B. Decap + Netlify Identity + Git Gateway** | Static **`/admin`** shell: **`public/admin/index.html`** loads Decap CDN + **`/admin/config.yml`** | **`backend.name: git-gateway`**, **`branch: main`**, **`site_url`** → **`https://empyrria-codex.netlify.app`** | **Full-field** Decap model vs Zierota Pages profile; **`invite.html`** + **`_redirect-identity.js`** support Identity **invite/recovery/confirmation** tokens. |

---

### 2. Canonical path for Zierota **now** (safest default)

**For routine, governance-hardened editorial (PATH A):** **Pages CMS** on branch **`pages-cms-prototype`** — **canonical constrained** surface per **EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK**.

---

### 3. Legacy fallback / higher-authority path

**Decap** at **`https://empyrria-codex.netlify.app/admin/`** (and related **`/admin/invite.html`**) with **Netlify Identity** + **Git Gateway** — **legacy rollback**, **higher-authority** full-field editing, and **Identity** email flows (**POST-MIGRATION** + **PAGES CMS VALIDATION** matrices). **Do not** assume **`https://empyrria-codex.pages.dev/admin/`** is **fully equivalent** for **Git Gateway**/**Identity** until **explicitly** re-validated against Netlify **`site_url`** and Identity settings.

---

### 4. Exact URL Zierota should use (operational)

- **PATH A (preferred):** Open **Pages CMS** for this repository with branch **`pages-cms-prototype`** — **entry** is via the team’s **Cloudflare Dashboard** → **Workers & Pages** → **Empyrria Codex** project → **Pages CMS** / content integration (**exact dashboard path is account-specific**). If the team uses the **hosted Pages CMS app**, **`https://app.pagescms.org`** is the **public** entry (then **sign in with GitHub** and select this repo + **`pages-cms-prototype`**).  
- **Fallback / full Decap:** **`https://empyrria-codex.netlify.app/admin/`** — use **Netlify Identity** as configured; **invite/recovery** links that land on **`/#…token…`** are routed by **`public/_redirect-identity.js`** (inlined in **`Layout.astro`**) to **`/admin/invite.html`** on the **same origin**.

---

### 5. Authentication method required

- **Pages CMS:** **GitHub** authentication and **repo write** access appropriate for **`pages-cms-prototype`**.  
- **Decap:** **Netlify Identity** (invite-based users) + **Git Gateway** to GitHub **`main`** per **`public/admin/config.yml`**.

---

### 6. Is GitHub access required?

- **Yes** for **Pages CMS** (PATH A).  
- **For Decap:** editors authenticate via **Netlify Identity**; **Git Gateway** still bridges to **GitHub** — maintainers need **Netlify**/**Identity** onboarding and **repo** permissions consistent with Git Gateway.

---

### 7. Is Cloudflare Pages CMS enough for PATH A editing?

**Yes** for the **locked** **PATH A** scope (**`title`**, **`meaning`**, **`facets`**, **`terms`** only) — **provided** **`npm run build`** / validation discipline after saves and periodic **readonly** round-trip checks (**PAGES CMS VALIDATION AUDIT — LOCK**). **Not** sufficient for **full** canon administration (doctrine, status/visibility edits, new rows, image workflow, etc.) without **Decap**/**git**/**ingestion** paths.

---

### 8. Is Decap / Netlify Identity still needed?

**Yes** today: **higher-authority** and **full-field** editorial; **rollback**; editors **without** a **GitHub-first** PATH A workflow; **Identity**-driven **invite/recovery**; **branch** posture (**Decap `main`** vs **`pages-cms-prototype`**) remains an **explicit unresolved dependency** in prior audits — **do not** retire until a **dedicated execution lock**.

---

### 9. Unsafe to remove right now

**Decap** bundle + **`public/admin/*`**; **`netlify.toml`**; **Netlify Identity** scripts and **`invite.html`**; **`public/_redirect-identity.js`** + **`Layout.astro`** inline hook; **`decap-cms-app`** dependency; **legacy Netlify** deployment — all **rollback / admin continuity** (**POST-MIGRATION LEGACY SYSTEM AUDIT — LOCK**).

---

### 10. Recommended next implementation step

**Non-destructive verification:** (1) Confirm **Zierota** can open **Pages CMS** from the **Cloudflare** project (or **`app.pagescms.org`**) and save a **trivial** **PATH A**-allowed edit on **`pages-cms-prototype`**, then **`npm run build`** green on PR. (2) Confirm **Decap** login still works on **`https://empyrria-codex.netlify.app/admin/`** after any **Identity** email flow. (3) **Do not** change **`site_url`** or **`backend.branch`** without a **governance + migration** lock addressing **main** vs **`pages-cms-prototype`** convergence.

---

### No-retirement boundary (explicit)

- **No** deletion or disabling of **Decap**, **Identity**, **`public/admin`**, **redirect** stack, or **Netlify** path until **POST-MIGRATION** + **PATH A** + **dedicated retirement execution lock** criteria are met.

### No-behavior-change statement

- **No** repository files, configs, permissions, **schema**, **`sigils.json`**, **routes**, **visibility**, or **deploy** settings were **modified** for this lock — **audit + master documentation only**.

---

## ZIEROTA EDITORIAL PRESSURE LOG — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-14)** — **documentation / operational-pressure logging / classification / governance framing only.** This phase is **observational**, **governance-aligned**, **operational-pressure collection**, and **classification-oriented**. It is **not** immediate implementation, schema rollout, CMS redesign, governance override, automatic feature approval, or cleanup execution.

**Strict boundary:** **No** **`.pages.yml`** edits, **no** schema edits, **no** runtime edits, **no** UI edits, **no** rendering fixes yet, **no** field removals yet, **no** relationship system implementation, **no** image upload implementation, **no** admin redesign, **no** cleanup or removal execution, **no** discoverability changes — **documentation and pressure taxonomy only.**

**Builds on:** **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW** (observe real friction; **no** implied governance-stack explosion), **EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK** (**PATH A**), **PAGES CMS VALIDATION AUDIT — LOCK**, **ZIEROTA ADMIN ACCESS — PHASE 1**, **POST-MIGRATION LEGACY SYSTEM AUDIT — LOCK**, **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (semantic boundary for relationship talk vs implementation).

**MASTER summary + condensed rules:** **`EMPYRRIA_MASTER.md`** → **ZIEROTA EDITORIAL PRESSURE LOG — PHASE 1**.

---

### 1. Purpose

**Why operational pressure logging exists:** Live **PATH A** use surfaces **real** editorial friction, schema appetite, rendering pain, and workflow expansion desires that **hypothetical** planning alone rarely captures. Logging them **in masters** preserves **traceability**, supports **prioritization**, and prevents **silent** scope creep through informal channel pressure.

**Real usage pressure vs hypothetical planning:** **Validated Zierota feedback** after **constrained Pages CMS** contact is **operational truth** for **what hurts now** or **what is wished for next** — it **does not** by itself define **what may ship** or **what may change** without later **execution locks** and **build**/**governance** gates.

**Stabilization-window alignment:** This log **implements** the observational half of **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW**: **major constitutional expansion** stays paused; **natural friction** from real editing and reading is **expected** and **healthy** to record.

**Observation-before-expansion philosophy:** Prefer **repeated**, **stable** operational need (or **clear** safety/readability harm) over **one-off** convenience or speculative field growth — align with **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** and **COMPATIBILITY-FIRST EVOLUTION** authoritative root.

---

### 2. Real operational feedback summary (Zierota — validated PATH A context)

The following items are **first-phase** operational signals from **Zierota** after **live PATH A** usage (Pages CMS on **`pages-cms-prototype`**, constrained profile). They are **logged**, not **approved** for work.

**Editorial expansion pressure**

- **Doctrine editing desire** — wish to adjust **`doctrine`** (and similarly **high-authority** prose blocks) from the same **routine** surface as **PATH A** metadata edits.  
- **New sigil creation desire** — wish to **add** new codex rows via CMS **without** going through the **ingestion / git** path.  
- **Image upload desire** — wish to attach or replace **plates** / **`image`** references **from** the editorial UI **without** a separate asset workflow.

**Field pressure** (desired or questioned **data** affordances, not implemented here)

- **Character Link** — associate sigils with **characters** or **personae**.  
- **Lore Context** — dedicated **lore** compartment beyond current **`meaning`** / **`layer`** / **`doctrine`** split.  
- **Sigil Relationships** — explicit **relationship** fields or edges (overlaps **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** semantics vs any **future** structured implementation).  
- **Place of Origin** — geographic or **provenance-of-symbol** register.

**Display / UX pressure** (public or admin **reading**/**editing** experience)

- **Editable main header** — control over the **primary** public heading (ceremonial **`title`** vs registry **`name`** vs route identity) from **editorial** flow.  
- **Preserve soft/hard enters** — **line breaks** and **paragraph** boundaries in long prose (**`doctrine`**, **`meaning`**, **`underlay`**) must survive **CMS → JSON → site** without collapsing to a **single** block.  
- **Rendering readability** — typographic / contrast / density improvements for **long-copy** legibility on detail surfaces.

**Cleanup pressure** (simplify **surfaces** or **model** — **observational** only; **no** execution in this phase)

- **`reviewReference`** — desire to **remove** or **hide** from editorial/public view.  
- **`deprecatedReason`** — desire to **remove** or **hide**.  
- **`archivedReason`** — desire to **remove** or **hide**.  
- **Remove colour logic** — reduce or drop **`color`** / classification colour semantics from **model** or **UI**.  
- **Remove associated terms** — reduce noise from **`terms`** (or related **chips**) in **display** or **data**.

---

### 3. Pressure classification table

Classifications are **primary** tags; many rows **touch** secondary domains (not duplicated in every cell). **PATH A safe** means “**could** be addressed **without** automatically violating **PATH A** **if** designed under a **future** lock” — **not** “approved to implement now.” **Separate lock** = **likely** **dedicated** governance or execution phase **before** shipping.

| Pressure item | Primary classification | Urgency (this phase) | Operational impact | Governance sensitivity | Safe for PATH A as-is? | Separate lock likely? |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Preserve paragraph / line breaks (soft vs hard enters) | Rendering; UX | **High** | Immediate trust in **long doctrine** fidelity | Low–medium (presentation vs canon integrity) | **Partially** (rendering may not require CMS change) | Possible **rendering-only** execution phase |
| Editable main / display header | UX; editorial workflow | **High** | Daily **orientation** and **ceremonial** correctness | Medium (authority of **`name`** vs **`title`**) | **No** (outside current **PATH A** editable set) | **Yes** |
| Rendering readability (typography, density, contrast) | Rendering; UX | **High** | Reader fatigue; **authority** of text **feels** weaker if illegible | Low–medium | **Yes** for **read-only** presentation tweaks | Optional **micro-pass** lock |
| Doctrine editing via constrained surface | Editorial workflow; governance | Medium | Core **canon** maintenance loop | **High** (**PATH A** explicitly excludes) | **No** | **Yes** |
| New sigil creation via CMS | Editorial workflow; schema; future architecture | Medium | **Ingestion** pipeline bypass risk | **High** | **No** | **Yes** |
| Image upload from CMS | Editorial workflow; schema; future architecture | Medium | Asset integrity; **build** gates; hosting | **High** | **No** | **Yes** |
| Character Link | Schema; editorial workflow; discoverability | Medium | Cross-entry **navigation** appetite | Medium–high | **No** | **Yes** |
| Lore Context field | Schema; editorial workflow | Medium | **Density** and **prose-first** tension (**SPARSE ENTRY** / **PROSE-PRESERVATION** roots) | Medium–high | **No** | **Yes** |
| Sigil Relationships (structured) | Schema; future architecture; governance | Medium | Intersects **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP** and **no graph** posture | **High** | **No** | **Yes** |
| Place of Origin | Schema; editorial workflow | Medium | **World** register growth | Medium | **No** | **Yes** |
| Hide/remove **`reviewReference`** | Cleanup; UX | Low | **Noise** in admin or detail | Medium (audit trail vs clutter) | **Unclear** (may be **readonly** governance) | **Yes** if data-affecting |
| Hide/remove **`deprecatedReason`** / **`archivedReason`** | Cleanup; governance | Low | Lifecycle **explainability** vs **minimal** UI | **High** (lifecycle **traceability**) | **No** without **CANON TRANSITION** alignment | **Yes** |
| Remove colour logic | Cleanup; schema; UX | Low | Simpler **Classification** block | Medium (existing **enrichment** history) | **No** for **schema** removal without lock | **Yes** |
| Remove associated **`terms`** / chips | Cleanup; discoverability; UX | Low | Quieter **surfaces**; less **wiki** velocity | Medium | **Partially** (display-only vs data) | **Maybe** |

---

### 4. High priority operational friction

**Likely cluster:** **Paragraph / line-break rendering** (soft vs hard enters), **editable display header** (ceremonial vs registry identity), **readability** improvements on detail surfaces.

**Clarification:** These items **hurt immediate usability** and **editorial confidence** in what readers see. Addressing them **later** may proceed through **small**, **isolated** execution phases and **does not** necessarily require **constitutional redesign** — but **this log does not authorize** any implementation.

---

### 5. Medium priority pressure

**Likely cluster:** **Image uploads**, **relationships**, **new sigil creation** via CMS, **lore context** fields, **character links**, **place of origin**.

**Clarification:** Each item **requires** **schema** and/or **workflow** design, **ingestion** alignment, and often **intersects** **PATH A** boundaries or **governance** locks (**CANON TRANSITION**, **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP**, **additive field** discipline). Evolution should be **careful**, **RFC-aligned**, and **gated** — **no** bulk rollout implied by listing them here.

---

### 6. Low priority / observational pressure

**Likely cluster:** **Legacy field** hiding or removal (**`reviewReference`**, **`deprecatedReason`**, **`archivedReason`**), **terminology** refinement, **colour** / **`terms`** simplification, **future admin** expansion.

**Clarification:** **Do not** optimize too early: some “**noise**” fields exist for **rollback**, **audit**, or **lifecycle honesty**. **Preserve** rollback and **admin continuity** (**POST-MIGRATION**) over **cosmetic** deletion until a **dedicated cleanup** lock weighs **traceability** vs **surface minimalism**.

---

### 7. Governance interpretation

- **Real usage pressure is valuable** — it **grounds** the roadmap in **editor** and **reader** reality under **PATH A**.  
- **Pressure does not equal automatic approval** — every line in **Section 2** remains **unauthorized work** until **explicit** execution phases.  
- **Requests reveal operational truth** — they show **where** the **constrained** model **bites**; they **do not** **override** **EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK**.  
- **Future implementation should emerge from repeated need** — prefer **pattern** over **single** impulse; align with **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE** “pressure detection” intent.  
- **Avoid speculative expansion** — do **not** treat this log as a **backlog mandate**; treat it as **classified telemetry** for **future** locks.

---

### 8. Stabilization window alignment

- **Validates the observational-governance model** — friction appeared **naturally** after real use; masters can **absorb** it **without** panic implementation.  
- **Real friction emerging is expected** — **PATH A** was chosen as **reduced scope**, not **pain-free** scope.  
- **Operational pressure is healthier than hypothetical complexity** — documented **real** wishes beat **undocumented** assumptions.  
- **Restraint remains active** — **this file** increases **visibility**, not **velocity**.

---

### 9. Future implementation boundary

- **Future fixes may be implemented incrementally** — one **theme** (e.g. **line breaks**) per **execution** phase where possible.  
- **Implementation requires isolated execution phases** — each **ship** needs its **own** lock or **RFC** gate as already practiced in **CODEX** implementation history.  
- **No bulk feature rollout implied** by this log.  
- **No schema explosion** — additive discipline (**COMPATIBILITY-FIRST EVOLUTION**, **SIGIL ENTITY TEMPLATE** / mapping plans) remains **binding context**, not superseded.  
- **No governance bypass** — **CANON TRANSITION**, **CANON EVIDENCE**, **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP**, and **PATH A** remain **authoritative** until **explicitly** amended by **traceable** locks.

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement (explicit)

- **No implementation executed** under this lock.  
- **No schema changes** to **`sigils.json`** or types.  
- **No UI changes** to Astro/components/CSS.  
- **No field removals** or data migrations.  
- **No relationship engine** or graph tooling.  
- **No image upload system** or asset pipeline expansion.  
- **No admin redesign** (Decap or Pages).  
- **No discoverability** or routing logic changes.  
- **Documentation / pressure classification only** — **canonical deployment** remains **Cloudflare Pages**; **PATH A** constrained **Pages CMS** remains active; **Decap**/**Netlify Identity** remain **preserved**; **governance locks** remain **authoritative**; **stabilization window** remains **in force**; **no canon transitions** are executed or implied by this phase.

## TEXT RENDERING & DISPLAY ERGONOMICS — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-14)** — **scoped presentation / UX micro-execution** on the **public** Astro surfaces. **Builds on** **ZIEROTA EDITORIAL PRESSURE LOG — PHASE 1** (high-priority friction: line breaks, headline, readability) and **EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK** (**PATH A** unchanged — **no** new editable fields).

**MASTER summary:** **`EMPYRRIA_MASTER.md`** → **TEXT RENDERING & DISPLAY ERGONOMICS — PHASE 1**.

---

### 1. Implementation scope (exact)

**In scope**

- **`src/lib/sigilDisplay.ts`**: new **`displayHeadline(sigil)`** — trimmed optional **`title`**, else trimmed **`name`**, else **`slug`**. **`toSigilDisplayItem`** uses **`displayHeadline`** for its **`title`** property (showcase and any **`SigilDisplayItem`** consumer).  
- **`src/pages/sigils/[slug].astro`**: detail **`<h1>`** and **`<Layout title>`** use **`displayHeadline`**; when headline differs from registry **`name`**, a **muted** secondary line shows **`name`** (internal/registry identity). Long-copy blocks use **`whitespace-pre-wrap`** + **`break-words`** (Tailwind) so JSON newlines render without HTML injection or Markdown.  
- **`src/components/SigilCard.astro`**: card title uses **`displayHeadline`**; doctrine preview **collapses** internal whitespace to a **single** line for grid density.  
- **`src/pages/showcase.astro`**: hero doctrine body uses **`whitespace-pre-wrap`**; grid doctrine preview collapses whitespace (existing ellipsis behavior).

**Out of scope (explicit)**

- **No** relationship system, graph, image upload, new sigil creation, doctrine editing via **PATH A**, **Decap**/**Netlify** cleanup, automation, broad redesign, **`.pages.yml`** edits, **`sigils.json`** or **Zod/TS schema** shape changes, visibility or routing logic changes, field removals, or slug behavior changes.

---

### 2. Fields affected (presentation only)

| Field / surface | Change |
| --- | --- |
| **`title`**, **`name`**, **`slug`** | **Headline** selection and optional **registry subtitle** on detail; **`<Layout title>`**; cards; **`toSigilDisplayItem().title`**. |
| **`meaning`** (explicit) | **`whitespace-pre-wrap break-words`** on detail. |
| **`doctrine`** | **`whitespace-pre-wrap break-words`** on detail; hero showcase; cards/showcase grid previews unchanged except **whitespace collapse** for truncation. |
| **`layer`** (explicit) | **`whitespace-pre-wrap break-words`** on detail. |
| **`usage`**, **`geometry`**, **`category`** | **`whitespace-pre-wrap break-words`** on detail. **`color`** was listed here originally; **public** Classification **colour** row **removed** in **EDITORIAL FIELD EVOLUTION — PHASE 1** (data retained). |
| **Underlay** (legacy line split + prototype lore/relations) | **Value** and **plain** lines: **`pre-wrap`** on spans/paragraphs so embedded newlines in a line survive. |
| **`relationsPreview`** | **`pre-wrap`**. |

**Rendering method:** Astro’s default **text** interpolation (HTML-escaped) + CSS **`white-space: pre-wrap`** via Tailwind **`whitespace-pre-wrap`**, plus **`break-words`** to reduce overflow on long tokens. **No** `set:html`, **no** Markdown pipeline added.

---

### 3. Display title fallback order

1. **`sigil.title`** (trimmed) if non-empty.  
2. Else **`sigil.name`** (trimmed) if non-empty.  
3. Else **`sigil.slug`**.

**Registry line on detail:** If **`name.trim()`** is non-empty **and** differs from the chosen **headline**, render **`name`** as the **muted** line under **`<h1>`** so **`title`**-as-headline still exposes stable registry identity. **`slug`** is **not** shown as a subtitle when used only as last-resort headline (edge case).

---

### 4. Authority, routing, visibility, schema

- **No canon authority change** — doctrine text is unchanged; only **how** it **wraps** changes.  
- **No routing change** — **`getStaticPaths`** and **`slug`** params unchanged.  
- **No visibility / discoverability change** — **`getPubliclyDiscoverableSigils`** / filters untouched.  
- **No schema explosion** — **no** new JSON keys in **TEXT RENDERING** phase; **subsequent** optional keys added only under **EDITORIAL FIELD EVOLUTION — PHASE 1** with additive schema + types.

---

### 5. Validation

- **`npm run build`** and **`npx astro check`** must pass before treating this phase as complete (record result in PR / commit notes).

---

### 6. Risks and follow-ups

- **`pre-wrap`** on **Underlay** may alter vertical rhythm vs old single-line chunks for values with many newlines — **acceptable** trade for fidelity; revisit under a **layout** lock if needed.  
- **Layer** field with **`uppercase` tracking** + multiple lines is rare; if awkward, a **future** micro-pass may relax typography for multi-line **`layer`**.  
- **Decap** list views (if any) are **unchanged** — only **site** rendering.

---

### 7. Amendment (EDITORIAL FIELD EVOLUTION — PHASE 1)

**Classification public surface:** **`color`** and **`terms`** are **no longer rendered** on **`/sigils/[slug]`** (see **EDITORIAL FIELD EVOLUTION — PHASE 1**). **`TEXT RENDERING`** **pre-wrap** rules for **`usage`** / **`geometry`** / **`category`** remain.

---

## EDITORIAL FIELD EVOLUTION — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-14)** — **controlled additive field evolution** + **public presentation cleanup** in service of **ZIEROTA EDITORIAL PRESSURE LOG — PHASE 1** medium-priority items, without **graph** tooling, **routing**/**visibility** changes, or **data deletion**.

**MASTER summary:** **`EMPYRRIA_MASTER.md`** → **EDITORIAL FIELD EVOLUTION — PHASE 1**.

---

### 1. Proposal record (pre-implementation design)

| Zierota label | Internal JSON key | Type | Public detail placement | PATH A editable | Decap |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Character Link | **`characterLink`** | string (textarea in CMS) | Section **Character link** after **Doctrine** (and other new blocks) | **Yes** | **Yes** (matching widget) |
| Lore Context | **`loreContext`** | string (textarea) | Section **Lore context** | **Yes** | **Yes** |
| Sigil Relationships | **`sigilRelationships`** | array of non-empty strings | Section **Sigil relationships** (bulleted; disclaimer line: declared labels only) | **Yes** | **Yes** (`list`) |
| Place of Origin | **`placeOfOrigin`** | string | Section **Place of origin** | **Yes** | **Yes** |

**Not done:** automatic inference, edges, graph UI, image upload, **`create: true`** for new sigils, doctrine unlocked on **PATH A**.

---

### 2. Schema and data

- **`src/types/sigil.ts`**: optional **`characterLink`**, **`loreContext`**, **`sigilRelationships`**, **`placeOfOrigin`**; governance keys (**`reviewReference`**, **`deprecatedReason`**, **`archivedReason`**, **`status`**, **`visibility`**, **`lastCanonReview`**) typed as optional on **`Sigil`** for JSON honesty.  
- **`src/data/sigils.schema.json`**: same keys added under **`$defs.sigil.properties`** (`additionalProperties: false` preserved).  
- **`src/data/sigils.json`**: corpus **`version`** bumped to **`11`**; **no** row keys deleted; new fields **omitted** until editorial use (additive).

---

### 3. Pages CMS (PATH A)

- **`.pages.yml`**: four new fields in the **Zierota-editable** band (with descriptions). **Readonly** governance fields unchanged.

---

### 4. Decap

- **`public/admin/config.yml`**: four widgets added to the sigil list (same semantics as **PATH A**). **No** removal of **`reviewReference`** / reason fields from admin (maintainers still need them).

---

### 5. Public display (`/sigils/[slug]`, showcase)

- **New:** render **`loreContext`**, **`characterLink`**, **`placeOfOrigin`**, **`sigilRelationships`** when non-empty; **`whitespace-pre-wrap break-words`** on prose fields.  
- **Hidden (public only):** **Colour logic** row and **Terms** row removed from **Classification**; **Indexing terms** disclosure removed for **top-iron-endurance**.  
- **`Lore (underlay)`** heading renamed from **“Lore context”** for the **underlay-split** prototype block to disambiguate from the **`loreContext`** field section.  
- **`reviewReference`**, **`deprecatedReason`**, **`archivedReason`**: were **never** rendered on public pages; remain **internal**/CMS only.  
- **`src/pages/showcase.astro`**: removed **Associated terms** line from grid cards.  
- **`src/lib/sigilDisplay.ts`**: **`toSigilDisplayItem().tags`** uses **`mergeTags(facets, undefined)`** so **terms** do not surface through the display adapter; **`empyrriaans`** no longer derives from **terms**.

---

### 6. Validation

- **`scripts/validate-content.mjs`**: type checks for new optional fields; **`sigilRelationships`** entries must be non-empty strings.

---

### 7. Explicit non-goals

- **No** field **deletion** from JSON rows.  
- **No** **`getPubliclyDiscoverableSigils`** / **`internal-test-fixture`** behavior change.  
- **No** canon transition automation.  
- **No** relationship **engine**.

---

### 8. Risks / follow-ups

- **`sigilRelationships`** is **presentation-only** — editors must treat entries as **labels**, not URLs, until a **future** linking lock.  
- **Duplicate lore** risk if both **`loreContext`** and underlay-split lore exist — acceptable; ordering is **Doctrine → editorial `loreContext` → … → underlay lore**.

---

## PATH A GOVERNANCE FIELD HIDING — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-14)** — **Pages CMS configuration only** (**`.pages.yml`**). **Builds on** **EDITORIAL FIELD EVOLUTION — PHASE 1** and **ZIEROTA EDITORIAL PRESSURE LOG — PHASE 1** (PATH A clutter).

**MASTER summary:** **`EMPYRRIA_MASTER.md`** → **PATH A GOVERNANCE FIELD HIDING — PHASE 1**.

---

### 1. Goal

Reduce **Zierota** **PATH A** (Pages CMS) **editor noise** from five fields that remain **required in data** and **available in Decap** / **git**, without touching **JSON**, **JSON Schema**, **Decap `config.yml`**, **content validator**, **public** Astro, **routing**, or **visibility** logic.

---

### 2. Exact files changed

| File | Change |
| --- | --- |
| **`.pages.yml`** | Added **`hidden: true`** to exactly five **`sigils`** nested field definitions (see below). |
| **`EMPYRRIA_MASTER.md`** | New lock section + cross-references. |
| **`EMPYRRIA_CODEX_MASTER.md`** | Implementation band, progress table row, this full section. |

**No other files** were modified in this phase.

---

### 3. Exact fields hidden (PATH A / Pages CMS only)

Under **`content` → `codex` → `fields` → `sigils` → `fields`**:

1. **`terms`** (Associated Terms)  
2. **`color`** (Color Logic)  
3. **`reviewReference`** (Review Reference)  
4. **`deprecatedReason`** (Deprecated Reason)  
5. **`archivedReason`** (Archived Reason)  

Each field block is **unchanged** except for the single added line **`hidden: true`** (no renames, type changes, **`readonly`** toggles, **`options`** / **`pattern`** / **`description`** edits, or removal of definitions).

---

### 4. What was not changed

- **`src/data/sigils.json`**, **`src/data/sigils.schema.json`**, **`public/admin/config.yml`**, **`scripts/validate-content.mjs`**  
- **Public Astro** (`src/pages/`, `src/components/`, `src/lib/`, layouts)  
- **`getPubliclyDiscoverableSigils`**, **`internal-test-fixture`**, **slug** routing, **canon** transition code  

---

### 5. Required validation

- **`npm run build`** (repo gate; **no** **`sigils.json`** shape change expected from this phase alone).  
- **Operational (post-deploy):** after the first **Pages CMS** save on a real sigil, **`git diff src/data/sigils.json`** (or PR diff) must show **no accidental removal** of the five keys’ values. If keys are stripped, **revert** **`.pages.yml`** and treat as **CMS round-trip** incident (see **Rollback**).

---

### 6. Rollback plan

Revert the commit that adds **`hidden: true`** to **`.pages.yml`** (and master doc pointers if reverting docs together). **Decap** and **JSON** remain authoritative for full-row edits throughout.

---

### 7. Result

- **PATH A:** five fields **no longer appear** in the Pages CMS editor UI (per [Pages CMS field `hidden`](https://pagescms.org/docs/configuration/content/fields/)).  
- **Data / governance continuity:** keys remain in **`sigils.json`** and **schema**; **Decap** still lists the same widgets; **validator** rules unchanged.  
- **Public site:** unchanged (this phase is **CMS profile** only).

## CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **governance-definition phase only.** Establishes **vocabulary** and **policy structure** for how codex **content** is expected to **change state** over time. **Does not** alter **`sigils.json`**, **schema**, **routes**, **discoverability** implementation, **Pages** / **Decap** configs, **search/filter** code, **packages**, or **archive file locations**. **Complements** **CANON INGESTION PIPELINE — LOCKED** (how entries **enter**) and **EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK** (**PATH A** — **which tool** may edit **which fields** today).

**Current reality preserved:** **Cloudflare Pages** = canonical public deployment; **PATH A** constrained **Pages CMS** remains the **Zierota** low-risk surface; **Decap + Identity** preserved as **higher-authority / fallback**; **live** visibility rules (**e.g.** **`getPubliclyDiscoverableSigils`**, **`provisional`** + **`marked_public`**) **unchanged** by this document; **no** canon migrations or retirement phases **started** here.

**Relationship to data fields:** Today’s **`status`**, **`visibility`**, and optional **`deprecatedReason`** / **`archivedReason`** keys are **implementation hooks**. This phase defines **conceptual** lifecycle and stability language; **mapping** hooks → lifecycle states for every row is a **future** documentation or schema pass — **not** executed in Phase **1**. **Who may approve tier moves and procedural escalation** are defined in **CANON TRANSITION GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (not in this vocabulary lock). **What counts as evidence and sufficient review when evaluating canon claims** — **CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (not in this vocabulary lock). **How interpretation, notes, and uncertainty may appear around canon without authority bleed** — **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (not in this vocabulary lock). **How conceptual relationships between entities may be described without implying equal canon authority** — **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (not in this vocabulary lock). **How governance documents themselves may evolve, supersede one another, and stay traceable** — **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (not in this vocabulary lock). **Where to find the consolidated constitutional index, domain map, and terminology guide across all governance locks** — **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1** (not in this vocabulary lock). **When the project intentionally pauses major governance expansion to observe operational friction** — **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW** (not in this vocabulary lock).

---

### 1. Content lifecycle model (formal categories)

These are **governance categories** — intent, authority, and stability expectations — **not** a mandate to rename keys in this phase.

| Category | Purpose | Visibility intent | Authority level | Expected stability | Editorial expectations |
| -------- | ------- | ------------------- | --------------- | ------------------- | ------------------------ |
| **Draft** | Work-in-progress text or structure **before** Zierota acceptance | Typically **non-public** or **internal** | **Low** — freely revisable **inside** the draft boundary | **Unstable** until promoted | **No** public discovery claims; **no** silent promotion to public without pipeline |
| **Provisional canon** | Approved-for-experiment **live** material; may gain density or polish | **Public candidate** when **`visibility`** policy allows (**e.g.** **`marked_public`**) | **Zierota** + **documented** review; **not** final “locked” tier | **Moderate** — refinements expected | **Transparent** that status is **provisional** in UI where applicable; **bounded** edits (**PATH A** fields on Pages; broader via **higher-authority** paths) |
| **Canon** | Zierota-recognized doctrine / identity for the library row | Per **`visibility`** + routing policy | **Zierota** **canon governance** | **High** — changes are **deliberate** | **Traceable** edits (PR, lock, or admin with rationale); **avoid** silent rewrites |
| **Deprecated** | Still **legible** but **disclaimed** — superseded, narrowed, or cautioned | May remain **addressable** or **discoverable** per policy — **not** “deleted” by label alone | **Governance review** to enter/exit | **Frozen** or **slow-changing** — movement toward archive or stable disclaimer | **Preserve** narrative value; **document** reason (**migration** of reader expectation, **not** erasure) |
| **Archived** | Withdrawn from active **promotional** posture; **historical** retention | Often **non-discoverable** or **clearly** archival in UI — policy-defined | **Governance** | **Low churn** — treat as **historical record** | **Do not** pretend archive is **invisible** to maintainers; **do** treat as **non-primary** canon pressure |
| **Internal** | Fixtures, tests, scaffolding, or ops-only rows | **Non-public** discovery | **Maintainers** | **Variable** | **Must not** pollute public narrative; **clear** separation from lore |
| **Hidden** | Intentionally **excluded** from browse/search surfaces while row may exist | **Suppressed** from **primary** discovery (implementation-specific) | **Governance + system** | **Stable** suppression rules | **Not** a license to bypass canon rules on **other** surfaces without policy |
| **Experimental** | Studies / branches / **`experiments/`** artifacts | **Non-canon** or **parallel** to public pack | **Exploratory** — does **not** auto-promote | **Unstable** | **Promotion** only via **ingestion pipeline** + locks — **see** **`canon/`** + **`EMPYRRIA_MASTER.md`** |
| **Historical artifact** | Frozen or **archive-grade** snapshot (e.g. checkpoint narrative, philosophy archive pointers) | **Reference** / **rollback** / **archaeology** | **Preservation** | **Append-only** or **rare** correction | **Narrative archaeology** valued — **edits** for **accuracy** only with **governance** |

---

### 2. Canon stability tiers (conceptual)

| Tier | What may change freely | What requires governance review | Historical preservation |
| ---- | ------------------------ | -------------------------------- | ------------------------ |
| **Unstable / exploratory** | Draft notes, experiments, **non-public** scratch | **Any** public-facing binding or slug identity | **Optional** capture as experiment artifact — **not** required for every scratch |
| **Soft canon** | **PATH A**-safe surface text (**`title`**, **`meaning`**, **`facets`**, **`terms`**) within **provisional** posture | **`doctrine`** shape, **`underlay`**, **`status`/`visibility`**, new **public** rows, **slug** | **Git history** + **locks** provide traceability |
| **Stable canon** | Same **PATH A** fields **with lighter** friction — still **build-gated** | **Structural** or **governance** moves (**deprecation**, tier shifts) | **Prefer** documented rationale fields when present |
| **Locked canon** | **Typo** / **clarity** fixes only under **explicit** mini-lock or Zierota directive | **Semantic** rewrites, **retcons** | **Diff-visible**; **no** silent “replace meaning” |
| **Historical canon** | **Errata**-class corrections | **Reinterpretation** that changes reader contract | **Preserve** prior reading where feasible (**append**, don’t **rewrite** history silently) |
| **Deprecated canon** | **Disclaimer** / **routing** metadata updates | **Removing** reader access without archive plan | **Keep** recoverable narrative where policy demands |

---

### 3. Review & maturation flow (concepts)

**Example transitions** (each future **execution** requires its **own** lock / PR / Zierota sign-off as applicable — **not** automated by Phase **1**):

| Transition | Typical trigger | Authority | Documentation expectation | Preservation |
| ---------- | ---------------- | --------- | -------------------------- | -------------- |
| **Draft → provisional / canon** | Zierota approval + **`canon/`** block + ingestion pipeline | **Canon governance** | **CANON INGESTION** + **CODEX** lock row | **Source** block remains **reference** |
| **Provisional → stable canon** | Review cadence satisfied; **atmosphere** / register coherence | **Canon governance** | Optional **`lastCanonReview`**-style note when used | **Prior** wording discoverable in **git** |
| **Canon → deprecated** | Supersession, scope narrowing, or safety disclaimer | **Governance review** | **`deprecatedReason`** (or equivalent) when field exists | **Row** or **redirect narrative** preserved per archive rules |
| **Deprecated → archived** | Withdrawal from active catalog pressure | **Governance** | **`archivedReason`** / archive section in masters | **Historical continuity** |
| **Internal → public candidate** | **Never** accidental — explicit promotion | **Canon governance** + **system** check (**build**, discoverability) | **Clear** first-public snapshot |

**Review triggers (non-exhaustive):** register drift signals (see **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE** observation targets); **overlap** pressure; **doctrine** tension across sigils; **new** public **slug**; **visibility** tier change.

---

### 4. Archive governance (philosophy)

- **Archives are preserved, not erased** — removal from **primary** navigation **≠** deletion from **history** or **git**.  
- **Deprecated material may remain historically valuable** — disclaimers **clarify** context; they **do not** strip all reference value.  
- **Old doctrine may remain searchable or referenceable** per **visibility** and **routing** policy — **archive ≠ deletion**.  
- **Historical continuity** supports **rollback**, **reader trust**, and **narrative archaeology** (understanding *why* text changed).  
- **Rollback / reference value:** tags, checkpoints, **`EMPYRRIA_PHILOSOPHY_ARCHIVE.md`**, and **commit history** are **part** of the archive story.

---

### 5. Public vs internal separation

| Layer | Operational intent | Boundary |
| ----- | ------------------- | -------- |
| **Public-facing lore** | **`sigils.json`** rows + assets intended for **discoverable** public routes | Governed by **`visibility`**, **`status`**, and **discoverability helpers** — **unchanged** in Phase **1** |
| **Internal experimentation** | **`internal`** fixtures, **non-public** **`visibility`**, **`experiments/`** studies | **Must not** be treated as **approved** public canon |
| **Governance-only material** | Masters, locks, RFCs, **`canon/`** approved blocks | **Authority** for **what** may enter JSON — **not** a substitute for **Zierota** |
| **Admin-only material** | **Decap**/**Identity** flows, invite URLs, **CMS** internals | **Operational** access — **does not** equal **canon** authority (**visibility ≠ authority**) |
| **Hidden reference structures** | **Suppressed** rows, **readonly** fields visible in CMS | **Editorial access** to read or **limited** write **≠** permission to **reclassify** canon without **governance** path |

---

### 6. Deprecation governance

| Topic | Definition |
| ----- | ---------- |
| **What deprecation means** | A **governance label** that a row or doctrine **no longer carries** the **same** reader contract — superseded, narrowed, or **cautionary**. |
| **What it does NOT mean** | **Not** “delete the file”; **not** “rewrite history as if it never existed”; **not** automatic **archived** state without **policy**. |
| **Preservation** | **JSON row**, **media**, and **reason** fields (when used) **remain** unless a **future** explicit retirement/migration lock says otherwise. |
| **Migration / reference** | Readers may be **guided** to replacements via **doctrine** text, **cross-links**, or **future** routing — **governed** separately. |
| **Canon continuity** | **New** reading coexists with **historical** reading where archives demand — **avoid** silent **retcon** across **stable** tiers. |

---

### 7. Editorial responsibility model (aligned with PATH A)

| Layer | Responsibility | Typical channels |
| ----- | ---------------- | ----------------- |
| **Constrained editorial surface** | **Low-risk**, **scoped** text/list refinement for allowed fields | **Pages CMS** (**PATH A** — **`title`**, **`meaning`**, **`facets`**, **`terms`**) |
| **Higher-authority editorial** | Full-row doctrine, **`underlay`**, **`image`**, governance metadata, **`slug`** lifecycle | **Decap** + **Identity** / **git** PRs per policy |
| **Canon governance** | What counts as **approved** public material, **ingestion**, **tier** promotion | **Zierota** + **`canon/`** + **CANON INGESTION PIPELINE** + **locks** |
| **Infrastructure governance** | Hosting, branches, CMS configs, schema, validators | **Dedicated** infra locks — **outside** **PATH A** |

**Tie-in:** **PATH A** **restricts** *tooling*; **Phase 1 lifecycle** **restricts** *meaning of state changes* — both must align before any **automation** or **schema** evolution.

---

### 8. Governance principles (explicit)

- **Preserve historical continuity** — prefer **append**, **disclaim**, **archive** over **silent removal**.  
- **Avoid silent canon rewrites** — especially at **stable** / **locked** tiers.  
- **Maintain traceability** — **git**, **locks**, **`deprecatedReason`** / **`archivedReason`** when used.  
- **Archives over deletion** — default stance for **deprecated** and **archived** narrative value.  
- **Governance before convenience** — faster CMS edit **≠** bypass review for **tier** changes.  
- **Visibility ≠ authority** — **public** or **hidden** in UI **does not** alone grant **canon** power.  
- **Editorial access ≠ canon authority** — **PATH A** editors **cannot** silently move **tiers** via readonly fields.  

---

### 9. Future-ready governance (platform-independent)

- **Tooling**, **schema**, and **UI** may **evolve** — this lifecycle model is meant to **survive** those changes.  
- **Pages CMS** and **Decap** are **implementation layers** for **editing** and **workflow** — **not** the **source of canon truth** (truth = **Zierota** + **approved sources** + **pipeline** + **locks**).  
- **Future** phases may: add **explicit enums**, UI for **tier** transitions, or **automation** — **only** under **new locks** after this vocabulary is **stable in practice**.

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** **`sigils.json`** content changed; **no** sigils **moved** between conceptual tiers **in data**.  
- **No** **`status`** / **`visibility`** values **modified** by this lock.  
- **No** editorial **permissions** or **discoverability** logic **changed**.  
- **No** migrations, **no** archive file moves, **no** route or search/filter edits.  
- **Governance definition only** — **operational** and **hosting** stance unchanged (**Cloudflare** canonical, **PATH A** Pages, **Decap/Identity** preserved). **Companion** transition-mechanics lock **CANON TRANSITION GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** data executed there). **Companion** evidence/review epistemology lock **CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** automation or canon verdicts). **Companion** annotation/commentary lock **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** commentary UI). **Companion** entity-relationship lock **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** graph implementation). **Companion** meta-governance lock **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** governance automation or permission changes). **Companion** consolidation/index lock **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** authority or **meaning** changes to prior locks).

---

## CANON TRANSITION GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **transition mechanics, authority, and procedural expectations only.** **Builds on** **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1** (lifecycle **vocabulary**, stability **tiers**, archive **philosophy**, principles). **This lock** specifies **who may move what**, **how deeply** transitions are reviewed, **preservation** during moves, **escalation**, and **traceability** — **not** new lifecycle **definitions**.

**Strict boundary:** **No** **`sigils.json`** edits, **no** **`status`**/**`visibility`** remapping, **no** discoverability or search/filter code changes, **no** CMS/admin/config/package/deploy edits, **no** workflow **automation** implemented. **Vocabulary** remains **conceptual**; **no** lifecycle automation exists; **no** canon transitions **executed** by this document.

**Epistemology (separate lock):** **What counts as evidence**, **what review depth is sufficient**, and **how interpretation differs from declaration** when **judging** transitions — **CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (this lock assumes those standards apply when **evaluating** proposals).

**Relationship to PATH A:** **PATH A** (**EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK**) permits **only** constrained field edits. **Tier moves**, **governance metadata** changes, **slug/public** promotion, **deprecation/archive** transitions, and **schema** work **exceed** **PATH A** unless a **separate** lock explicitly authorizes a **narrow** exception.

**Meta-governance (separate lock):** **How** governance **locks**, **constitutional** posture, and **operational** guidance may **amend** or **supersede** one another **without** **silent** authority escalation or **erased** history — **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**.

**Constitutional index (separate lock):** **Where** each governance **domain** lives, **how** locks **relate**, and **preferred** **terminology** — **without** **redesigning** rules — **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1**.

---

### 1. Transition authority model

| Authority layer | Who may **suggest** | Who may **approve** / **execute** | What requires **governance review** | Must stay **outside** ordinary PATH A editing |
| ----------------- | ------------------- | ---------------------------------- | ----------------------------------- | ----------------------------------------------- |
| **Constrained editorial surface** (Pages **PATH A**) | Editors with **GitHub** access on the working branch | **Same** path for **allowed** fields only — **self-approve** at **low** tier **only** for **`title`**, **`meaning`**, **`facets`**, **`terms`** | **Cross-sigil** tone or register impact when **material** — use **CODEX** audits / Zierota check | **`status`**, **`visibility`**, **`slug`**, **`doctrine`**, **`underlay`**, **`image`**, archive reasons, **schema** |
| **Higher-authority editorial** (Decap / **git** PR) | Trained editors / maintainers | **Zierota** or **delegated** maintainer per project practice; **PR** review for **git** | **Full-row** doctrine changes; **`underlay`**; **image** path changes; **governance** fields when config allows | **Still not** a substitute for **canon governance** on **new public canon** without **`canon/`** + ingestion |
| **Canon governance** | Anyone may **propose** via agreed channel | **Zierota** (or **explicit** written delegate recorded in masters/PR) | **New** public rows; **promotion** to stronger tiers; **contradiction** resolution policy; **deprecation** intent | **Invented** lore; **silent** tier jumps |
| **Governance locks** (masters) | Maintainers draft | **Lock** text reflects **approved** scope — treat as **binding** for the phase | Any **codex-wide** rule change, **execution** of retirement/migration, **CMS** scope expansion | **Opportunistic** edits that contradict an active **LOCK** |
| **Infrastructure governance** | Maintainers | **Dedicated** infra lock + owners | **Hosting**, **branch**, **schema**, **validators**, **routes** | **Content** editors acting **without** infra lock |

**Summary:** **Suggest** ≠ **approve** for **tier** and **visibility**-impacting work. **PATH A** **never** **solely** approves **canon-impacting transitions**.

---

### 2. Lifecycle transition rules (procedural)

States are defined in **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1** §1–§2. Below: **intent**, **review depth**, **preservation**, **reversibility** for **governance** (future execution must still follow **locks** + **ingestion**).

| Transition | Intent | Expected review depth | Preservation during move | Reversibility |
| ---------- | ------ | ---------------------- | -------------------------- | -------------- |
| **Draft → provisional canon** | Enter **pipeline** toward **public** experiment | **Full** — **`canon/`** approval + **CANON INGESTION** + build | Keep **draft** history in **git**; **source** block is **anchor** | **N/A** (forward pipeline); **revert** via **git** if error **before** public lock-in |
| **Provisional canon → canon** (stronger tier) | Reduce **uncertainty**; stabilize reader contract | **Deep** — see §3 | **Append** clarifications; **avoid** wholesale replace | **Discouraged** to **downgrade** casually; reversal = **new** governed transition |
| **Canon → deprecated** | Disclaim / supersede without **erasing** | **Governance** + documented **rationale** | **Retain** row + text; **add** disclaimer fields when used | **Partially** reversible (undeprecate) **only** with **governance** + rationale |
| **Deprecated → archived** | Withdraw from **active** catalog pressure | **Governance** | **Retain** narrative for **archaeology**; adjust **discovery** only under **future** implementation + lock | **Low** — treat as **serious** |
| **Internal → public candidate** | Controlled **promotion** | **Highest** — ingestion + **visibility** policy + **build** | **No** leakage of **internal** tone into **public** voice | **Reversible** to internal **only** via **governed** rollback (not silent) |
| **Experimental → historical artifact** | Freeze **study** for reference | **Light** if already non-canon; **doc** link from **canon** if cited | **Keep** **`experiments/`** or archive pointer | **Stable** — prefer **new** experiment fork |

---

### 3. Canon promotion governance (preconditions)

Before **promotion** into a **stronger** canon tier (**soft → stable**, **provisional → canon**, etc.), **expect** (non-exhaustive — **future** execution may add checklists):

- **Review expectations:** at least one **cross-read** for **register** fit (**DOCTRINAL REGISTER** audits as model).  
- **Stability expectations:** **build** + **content validate** pass; **no** known **blocking** contradictions **unrecorded**.  
- **Contradiction review:** overlapping sigils **named**; **coexistence** or **scoped** claim **documented** (see §6).  
- **Doctrine consistency:** **no** accidental **genre** or **power** drift vs **atmosphere** locks.  
- **Reference verification:** **`canon/`** block, **`reviewReference`** (when field used), **media** paths real.  
- **Historical continuity checks:** prior wording **recoverable**; **no** silent **retcon** at **locked** tier.  
- **Governance lock requirements:** **material** promotions **should** pair with a **CODEX** lock row or **explicit** PR description recorded in masters — **not** “JSON-only drift.”  

---

### 4. Locked canon governance (protection)

- **Locked canon** **resists casual edits** — **typo**/format fixes may be **allowed** under **mini**-scope; **semantic** edits require **escalation** (§7).  
- **Modifications require governance escalation** — **Zierota** or **stewardship** decision + **traceable** diff.  
- **Preserve historical continuity** — prefer **additive** clarification, **footnotes-in-prose**, or **paired** deprecation over **destructive** replacement.  
- **Avoid silent rewrites** — if meaning shifts, **reader** should **see** governance signal (**version** bump, lock, **deprecated** sibling, etc.) per **future** policy.  
- **Prefer additive clarification over destructive replacement** at **stable/locked** tiers.  

---

### 5. Deprecation / archive transitions (mechanics)

| Topic | Rule |
| ----- | ---- |
| **Triggers** | Superseding doctrine, **safety** narrowing, **register** cleanup, **Zierota** strategic withdrawal from **active** catalog — **not** “mild dislike.” |
| **Archive entry expectations** | **`archivedReason`** / master note when fields exist; **CODEX** / **MASTER** **lock** or **audit** row for **codex-wide** posture changes. |
| **Historical retention** | **Row** and **media** **preserved** unless a **future** **execution** lock authorizes removal — default **retain**. |
| **Migration / reference** | **Guide** readers to replacement via **prose**, **cross-links**, or **future** routing — **governed** separately from **label** change. |
| **Preservation of old references** | **URLs** / **slugs** **stable** policy: **do not** break **identity** without **redirect** or **lock** strategy (**infrastructure** §). |
| **Historical doctrine handling** | **Deprecated** text may **remain** **readable**; **annotate** context rather than **purge**. |

---

### 6. Conflict & contradiction governance

- **Contradictory doctrine:** prefer **coexistence** with **scoped** claims + **annotation** over **winner-takes-all** deletion — unless **Zierota** mandates **replacement** under **lock**.  
- **Overlapping sigils:** **explicit** **register** positioning; **enrichment** passes as **precedent** for **single-sigil** resolution scope.  
- **Competing interpretations:** **may** **coexist** as **layers** (**meaning** vs **`doctrine`** depth) if **atmosphere** holds; **else** escalate to **canon governance**.  
- **Historical revisions:** **preserve** **branch** in **git**; **masters** record **decision** rationale.  
- **Unresolved canon tensions:** **document** “**unresolved**” in **governance** text **or** **internal** note — **do not** fake closure.  
- **Coexistence vs replacement** — default **coexistence** + **clarify**; **replacement** requires **strong** review.  
- **Annotation vs deletion** — default **annotation**.  
- **Historical branch preservation** — **no** **force-pushed** history rewrite for **governance** convenience (**infra** policy).  

---

### 7. Governance escalation model

| Level | Examples | Formal **lock** in masters? | **PATH A** sufficient alone? |
| ----- | -------- | --------------------------- | ---------------------------- |
| **L1 — Ordinary editorial change** | **PATH A** fields; typo in **non-locked** prose via **git** | **No** if scope **tiny** and **reversible** | **Yes** (within allowed fields) |
| **L2 — Governance review required** | **Meaning** shift affecting **register**; cross-sigil **tone** | **Recommended** — audit or **mini-lock** | **No** for **tier** implications |
| **L3 — Canon-impacting transition** | **Promotion**, **deprecation**, **new public slug**, **`visibility`** change | **Yes** — **dedicated** lock row or **ingestion** lock | **No** |
| **L4 — Infrastructure-impacting transition** | **Schema**, **routes**, **discoverability**, **branch** | **Yes** — **infra** lock | **No** |
| **L5 — Historical preservation review** | **Locked** tier edit, **archive** of **widely cited** doctrine | **Yes** + **stewardship** posture | **No** |

**Rules:** **What requires formal locks:** **L3–L5** always; **L2** when **audit** flags **pressure** or **overlap**. **What remains editorial-only:** **L1** within **PATH A** / **small** **git** fixes. **What exceeds PATH A:** **all** **`status`**/**`visibility`**/**`slug`**/**`doctrine`**/**`underlay`**/**`image`** transitions and **any** **tier** move.

---

### 8. Traceability principles

- **Transition traceability** — every **tier** move **should** leave: **git** commit, **PR** description, and/or **CODEX** lock row.  
- **Historical visibility** — **readers** and **maintainers** can **reconstruct** “**what** changed **when**” without **secret** edits.  
- **Preservation of prior states** — **git** is **default** archive; **optional** reason fields capture **intent**.  
- **Governance transparency** — **locks** state **scope** and **non-goals** clearly (**no** hidden parity creep).  
- **Rationale preservation** — **`deprecatedReason`**, **`archivedReason`**, **`reviewReference`** when used; **masters** for **codex-wide** decisions.  
- **Avoiding invisible canon drift** — **forbid** **long** **undeclared** **semantic** drift on **stable**/**locked** rows; **batch** changes need **visible** governance.  

---

### 9. Future implementation boundary

- **Transitions are conceptual / procedural first** — this document **does not** implement **buttons**, **validators**, or **enums**.  
- **Future tooling** may **assist** (UI wizards, **schema** enums, **CI** checks) — **must not** **auto-approve** **Zierota** decisions.  
- **Automation must not replace governance authority** — **CI** can **block** mistakes; **cannot** **grant** canon.  
- **Mechanics remain platform-independent** — same rules if **Pages**, **Decap**, or **plain git** **wins** long-term.  

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** **`status`** values changed; **no** **`visibility`** or discoverability logic changed.  
- **No** sigils **promoted**, **deprecated**, or **archived** **in data** by this lock.  
- **No** **CMS** permissions, **Decap** config, or **Pages** **`.pages.yml`** edits.  
- **No** workflow **automation** or **migrations** added.  
- **Governance / process definitions only** — **Cloudflare** canonical deployment, **PATH A** Pages, **Decap/Identity** preserved; **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1** vocabulary **unchanged** in **meaning** (this lock **adds transition mechanics** only — **not** new lifecycle definitions). **Companion** evidence/review epistemology lock **CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** data or automation). **Companion** annotation/commentary lock **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** commentary UI). **Companion** entity-relationship lock **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** graph implementation). **Companion** meta-governance lock **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** governance automation). **Companion** consolidation/index lock **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** constitutional **redefinition**).

---

## CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **evidence taxonomy, review epistemology, and canon-evaluation standards only.** **Builds on** **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1** (vocabulary / stability **language**), **CANON TRANSITION GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (authority / **when** moves may occur). **This lock** answers: **what counts as evidence**, **what “sufficient review” means**, how **confidence** in canon is judged, how **interpretation** differs from **declaration**, and how **conflicting evidence** is held without **false closure**.

**Strict boundary:** **No** **`sigils.json`**, **no** **schema**, **no** **`status`**, **`visibility`**, or discoverability changes, **no** CMS/admin/deploy/package edits, **no** **review automation** or **CI** “canon verdict” implementation. **Lifecycle / transitions** remain **conceptual** as before; **no** canon transitions **executed** here.

**Annotation & commentary (separate lock):** **How** notes, **symbolic** readings, and **uncertainty** may **surround** declared canon **without** **silent** **authority** **mutation** — **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**.

**Entity relationships (separate lock):** **How** conceptual **links** between sigils, doctrine, layers, and symbols are **governed** **without** **graph** edges **becoming** **undeclared** doctrine — **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**.

**Meta-governance (separate lock):** **How** the **governance corpus** itself **evolves** — **amendment** authority, **supersession**, **hierarchy**, and **preservation** of prior governance **reasoning** — **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**.

**Constitutional index (separate lock):** **Cross-lock** **navigation**, **terminology**, and **dependency** map — **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1**.

---

### 1. Canon evidence model (taxonomy)

Evidence is **graded**, not binary. **Context** (which sigil, which register, which **tier**) changes weight.

| Evidence category | Relative reliability (typical) | Authority expectations | Contextual interpretation |
| ----------------- | -------------------------------- | ------------------------ | ------------------------- |
| **Direct doctrine declaration** | **High** when it is **explicit** Zierota-approved text in **`canon/`** mirrored in **`sigils.json`** | **Canon governance** owns contradiction with other **approved** blocks | Read in **register** context; **sparse** entries remain valid |
| **Canon lock / governance statements** | **High** for **process** and **scope**; **medium** for **fine-grained lore** unless locks cite **canon** | **Locks** bind **phase** work — **do not** invent lore **beyond** lock text | **Temporal** — later lock may **narrow** earlier **intent** only via **governed** change |
| **Recurring symbolic patterns** | **Medium** as **heuristic** — **not** automatic proof | **Audits** may **flag** pressure; **Zierota** decides **elevation** | **Repetition ≠ confirmation** (see §7) |
| **Stable historical references** | **High** for **continuity**; **variable** for **new claims** | **Git** + **masters** as **artifact** trail | Distinguish **“was said”** vs **“is still binding”** |
| **Narrative consistency** | **Medium–high** — **cross-sigil** coherence checks | **Governance review** / audits | **Coherence** can **disprove** careless edits; **rarely** **proves** hidden lore alone |
| **Authored explanatory notes** | **Medium** — **meta** or **editorial** gloss | **Subordinate** to **`canon/`** + **`doctrine`** unless **promoted** | Treat as **annotation** unless **declared** (§2) |
| **Archival references** | **High** for **history**; **low** alone for **current** binding | **Philosophy archive**, checkpoints, **experiments/** | **Historical** ≠ **current canon** unless **re-ingested** |
| **Implementation artifacts** | **High** for **system behavior**; **low** for **lore truth** | **Code** shows **what ships** — **not** what **Zierota** **meant** | **Tooling state ≠ authority** (§7) |
| **Contradictory evidence** | **Valid** as **data** — forces **explicit** resolution strategy | **Must not** be **suppressed** silently | Prefer **documented** coexistence, **scoped** claims, or **deprecation** path (§5) |
| **Unresolved interpretation** | **Neutral** — absence of proof | **May remain** under **governance** choice | **Ambiguity** can be **intentional** (§2, §5) |

---

### 2. Declaration vs interpretation

| Concept | Definition | Governance rule |
| ------- | ---------- | ----------------- |
| **Explicitly declared canon** | **`canon/`**-backed (or **equivalent** Zierota **written**) **commitment** carried into **`sigils.json`** / public routes per **ingestion** | **Only** this tier **binds** the **library** as **approved Empyrria** material |
| **Inferred interpretation** | Reader or maintainer **derivation** from patterns, tone, or **sparse** hints | **Not** automatically canon — requires **declaration** path to **promote** |
| **Symbolic implication** | Suggestive geometry, color, **facet** names — **evocative** | **Atmosphere** asset — **not** **standalone** proof of **new** lore claims |
| **Speculative association** | “**Could** mean X” without **approved** text | **Out of band** for **public** certainty — belongs in **experiments/** or **internal** discussion |
| **Unresolved reading** | Multiple **coherent** readings **remain** | **May stay** **open** — **document** tension rather than **force** closure |

**Rules:** **Interpretation is not automatically canon.** **Recurring symbolism is not automatic confirmation.** **Ambiguity may remain intentionally unresolved** when **atmosphere** or **honesty** prefers it.

---

### 3. Review confidence levels (conceptual)

| Level | Evidence / review expectation | Contradiction tolerance | May remain unresolved? |
| ----- | ------------------------------ | ------------------------ | ------------------------ |
| **Uncertain** | **Thin** evidence; **hypothesis** stage | **High** — expect **revision** | **Yes** |
| **Exploratory** | **Directed** experiments; **non-public** or **clearly** scoped | **High** | **Yes** |
| **Provisional** | **`canon/`** + **ingestion** + **build**; **marked** as **provisional** in policy | **Moderate** — **refinement** expected | **Yes** for **fine** detail |
| **Reviewed** | **Cross-read** + **audit** hooks (**register**, repetition, overlap) as applicable | **Low–moderate** | **Minor** tensions **documented** |
| **Stable** | **Strong** evidence bundle + **time** / **stewardship** without **contradiction** **surprises** | **Low** | **Only** **named** **residual** tensions |
| **Locked** | **Zierota** **explicit** stability intent + **governance** | **Very low** — **typo**-class only without escalation | **Rarely** — **dispute** → **historically disputed** |
| **Historically disputed** | **Competing** **declarations** or **readings** over **time** | **Managed** via **annotation**, **layers**, or **deprecation** | **Yes** — **honesty** preserved |

**Stable / locked** material **requires** **stronger** evidence and **deeper** review than **provisional** (**aligns** with **CANON TRANSITION** §3–§4).

---

### 4. Review expectation model

**Review may include** (non-exhaustive; **depth scales** with **canon impact** per **CANON TRANSITION** escalation):

- **Doctrine consistency** — internal logic + **cross-sigil** register fit.  
- **Historical continuity** — **git** / **masters** / **`canon/`** alignment; **no** silent **retcon**.  
- **Contradiction analysis** — **map** tensions; choose **coexistence**, **scope**, **deprecation**, or **unresolved** record.  
- **Symbolic coherence** — **atmosphere** / **sparse-entry** rules; **not** **density** mandates.  
- **Lifecycle alignment** — proposed change **fits** **CONTENT** vocabulary + **CANON TRANSITION** authority.  
- **Archive reference checks** — deprecated/archived **still** **legible** where policy requires.  
- **Prior-lock compatibility** — **no** **active** **LOCK** violated without **new** lock.  
- **Implementation consistency** — **build**, **validators**, routes **match** **declared** **visibility** (when **infra** phase runs).

**Rule:** **Higher** impact → **more** evidence + **wider** review surface + **stronger** traceability (§8).

---

### 5. Contradictory evidence governance (epistemology)

- **Conflicting doctrine** — treat both texts as **evidence** until **Zierota** picks **scoped** coexistence, **replacement**, or **layered** reading; **annotation** preferred over **silent replacement**.  
- **Conflicting interpretations** — **may** **coexist** as **non-declared** **readings**; **only** **declaration** path **binds** the **library**.  
- **Historical inconsistencies** — **preserve** the **record**; **errata**-style correction **over** **pretend** uniformity.  
- **Layered meanings** — **valid**; **disclose** **layer** (e.g. **meaning** vs **`doctrine`**) where helpful.  
- **Intentional ambiguity** — **governance** may **choose** **not** to **collapse** readings.  
- **Unresolved contradictions** — **document** in **governance** text or **review** notes — **not** **hidden**.  

**Principles:** **Contradictory records may coexist historically.** **Uncertainty may remain preserved.** **Annotation > silent replacement** (consistent with **CANON TRANSITION** §6).

---

### 6. Historical evidence philosophy

- **Older material may retain value** — as **context**, **counterpoint**, or **archaeology**.  
- **Archived doctrine may still inform interpretation** — as **historical** voice, **not** as **silent** **current** **law** unless **re-declared**.  
- **Historical artifacts may preserve abandoned meanings** — **experiments/**, **checkpoints**, **archive** docs.  
- **Deprecated ≠ erased from historical memory** — **reader** and **maintainer** **memory** + **git** **remain**.  

---

### 7. Canon stability epistemology

- **Stability derives from** **review** + **continuity** + **consistency** — **not** from **heat** or **volume**.  
- **Popularity / visibility ≠ canon strength** — **public** rows **≠** **doctrinal certainty**.  
- **Editorial repetition ≠ proof** — **reuse** of phrases **flags** **audit**; **does not** **elevate** **speculation**.  
- **Tooling state ≠ authority** — **what the CMS allows** **≠** what **Zierota** **declared**.  
- **Public exposure ≠ doctrinal certainty** — **marketing** or **routing** **errors** **must not** **upgrade** **confidence** without **evidence** (§1–§3).  

---

### 8. Review traceability
