- **Rationale preservation** — **PR** bodies, **`reviewReference`**, **`deprecatedReason`**, **`archivedReason`**, **lock** rows.  
- **Governance references** — cite **which** **CONTENT** / **TRANSITION** / **EVIDENCE** standard applied.  
- **Lock references** — **which** **LOCK** authorized **scope** (or **explicit** Zierota communique recorded).  
- **Historical review notes** — **append** **why** **confidence** changed — **not** **only** **that** JSON changed.  
- **Preserving why transitions occurred** — ties to **CANON TRANSITION** §8; **epistemic** **why** **adds** **evidence** **story** for **future** readers.  

---

### 9. Future implementation boundary

- **Tooling** may **assist** review workflows (diffs, **lint** for **missing** **`canon/`** links, dashboards) — **governance-defined** thresholds **first**.  
- **Automation may surface evidence** (contradiction **detectors**, **n-gram** **flags**) — **must not** **determine** canon or **auto-merge** **declarations**.  
- **Evidence standards remain governance-defined** — **CI** **cannot** **lower** the **bar** without a **lock**.  
- **Epistemology survives** **platform** changes — **Pages** / **Decap** / **plain git** **irrelevant** to **what counts as proof**.  

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** canon **states** in **data** changed; **no** sigils **promoted** / **deprecated** / **archived** by this lock.  
- **No** discoverability or **visibility** logic changed; **no** **permissions** changed.  
- **No** **review automation** or **schema** added.  
- **Governance definitions only** — **Cloudflare** canonical deployment, **PATH A** Pages, **Decap/Identity** preserved; **lifecycle**/**transition** locks **unchanged** in **role** (this lock **adds epistemology** only). **Companion** annotation/commentary lock **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** commentary system shipped). **Companion** entity-relationship lock **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** graph). **Companion** meta-governance lock **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** autonomous governance edits). **Companion** consolidation/index lock **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** meaning drift).

---

## CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **annotation philosophy, commentary boundaries, and representation rules only.** **Builds on** **CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (declaration vs interpretation, evidence grading), **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1** (lifecycle / archive posture), **CANON TRANSITION GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** (who executes tier moves). **This lock** governs **layers of speech** **around** canon — **not** new evidence **taxonomy** (see **CANON EVIDENCE**) and **not** transition **execution**.

**Strict boundary:** **No** **`sigils.json`**, **no** **schema**, **no** **data** edits, **no** **`status`**/**`visibility`** or discoverability/search changes, **no** **CMS** configs, **no** **annotation UI** or **comment** system implementation, **no** **automation** that **promotes** commentary to canon, **no** deploy/package edits.

**Current reality preserved:** **Cloudflare** canonical deployment; **PATH A** Pages; **Decap/Identity** preserved; prior governance locks remain **conceptual** where stated; **no** annotation tooling exists; **no** canon transitions executed by this document.

**Entity relationships (separate lock):** **How** conceptual **links** (sigil↔sigil, doctrine↔layer, symbol↔archive) are **governed** **without** **graph** edges **becoming** **undeclared** doctrine — **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**.

**Meta-governance (separate lock):** **How** governance **documents** may **change** while **preserving** **supersession** trail and **constitutional** continuity — **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**.

**Constitutional index (separate lock):** **Domain**/**terminology** map for readers — **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1**.

---

### 1. Annotation model (taxonomy)

Annotations **supplement** canon — they **do not** **silently** **replace** or **upgrade** **declared** authority. They **may** **coexist** with **uncertainty**.

| Annotation / contextual type | Typical role | Authority | Coexists with uncertainty? |
| ---------------------------- | ------------- | --------- | --------------------------- |
| **Editorial notes** | Craft, cadence, **register** hints | **Low** — **maintainer** voice | **Yes** |
| **Historical notes** | **When** / **why** text existed; **checkpoint** refs | **Medium** for **facts**; **low** for **binding** lore | **Yes** |
| **Interpretation commentary** | Reader-facing **gloss** on **meaning** | **Low** unless **promoted** via **canon** path | **Yes** |
| **Contradiction annotations** | **Flags** tension; **points** to **coexistence** strategy | **Documentary** — **not** a **verdict** alone | **Yes** |
| **Symbolic observations** | Pattern, geometry, color **readings** | **Heuristic** — **CANON EVIDENCE** §1 | **Yes** |
| **Unresolved questions** | **Honest** **open** threads | **Neutral** | **Yes** — **preferred** to **false** closure |
| **Archive context** | **Why** material lives in **archive** posture | **Governance** narrative | **Yes** |
| **Implementation notes** | **Build**, routing, **CMS** behavior | **High** for **system**; **low** for **lore truth** | **N/A** |
| **Governance references** | Pointers to **locks**, **RFCs**, **audits** | **High** for **process** | **Yes** |
| **Review commentary** | **PR** / **lock** discussion, **rationale** | **Medium** — **traceability** anchor | **Yes** |

---

### 2. Canon vs commentary separation

| Layer | Definition | Rule |
| ----- | ---------- | ---- |
| **Canon declaration** | **`canon/`**-backed + **ingested** **doctrine** / identity fields **approved** as **public** canon | **Only** layer that **binds** the **library** as **Zierota-approved** Empyrria material |
| **Commentary** | **Explanatory**, **interpretive**, or **meta** text **explicitly framed** as **non-declarative** | **Does not** automatically **become** canon |
| **Interpretation** | **Derived** reading — may live in **meaning** band, **footnotes**, **future** **annotation** UI | **Contextual** — **CANON EVIDENCE** §2 |
| **Speculation** | **Hypothesis** without **approved** backing | **Must not** **masquerade** as **doctrine** |
| **Historical note** | **Past** state, **abandoned** reading, **checkpoint** | **Preserves** **memory** — **not** **silent** **current** **law** |
| **Symbolic analysis** | **Pattern** commentary | **Atmosphere** asset — **not** **auto-proof** |
| **Governance rationale** | **Why** a **lock** or **transition** occurred | **Binds** **process** — **not** **new** **lore** unless **declared** |

**Clarifications:** **Commentary does not automatically become canon.** **Explanatory notes ≠ doctrinal declaration.** **Visibility** of commentary (**future**) **≠** **authority** (**CANON EVIDENCE** stability epistemology).

---

### 3. Uncertainty representation

- **Unresolved interpretation** — may **remain** **visible** in **annotation** or **governance** text.  
- **Disputed reading** — **document** **sides**; **avoid** **pretend** **unanimity**.  
- **Contradictory evidence** — **hold** both as **evidence**; **annotate** relation (**CANON EVIDENCE** §5).  
- **Symbolic ambiguity** — may be **intentional** **atmospheric** **reserve**.  
- **Incomplete historical context** — **state** **gap** rather than **invent** **fill**.  

**Principles:** **Uncertainty may remain intentionally visible.** **Ambiguity is not always a defect.** **Unresolved interpretation may coexist with stable canon** — **stability** is about **declared** **tier** + **review**, **not** about **erasing** **all** **tension** in **commentary** space.

---

### 4. Commentary authority levels (hierarchy)

**Higher** binds **more** — **commentary layers** are **contextual** and **default** **subordinate** to **canon** + **Zierota**.

| Layer | Relative authority | Notes |
| ----- | ------------------- | ----- |
| **Canon declarations** | **Highest** for **lore** **truth** claims | **Ingestion** path |
| **Governance locks** | **Highest** for **phase scope** / **process** | **Do not** invent **undeclared** lore |
| **Editorial notes** | **Low** | **Stylistic** / **craft** |
| **Symbolic interpretations** | **Low–medium** | **Heuristic** only |
| **Archive annotations** | **Medium** for **history**; **subordinate** for **current** **law** | **Deprecated** text **still** **teaches** **context** |
| **Implementation observations** | **High** for **system**; **irrelevant** alone for **canon** **promotion** | **Tooling ≠ authority** |
| **Speculative commentary** | **Lowest** for **binding** claims | **Label** clearly |

---

### 5. Historical commentary governance

- **Commentary on archived / deprecated material** — **should** **explain** **posture** (**why** deprecated) **without** **purging** **prior** **readings**.  
- **Preservation of older interpretations** — **git**, **masters**, **archive** docs **retain** **evidence** of **how** readers **saw** text.  
- **Historical review notes** — **append** **why** **readings** **shifted**.  
- **Evolving readings over time** — **new** **commentary** **layers** **stack**; **avoid** **retroactive** **pretense** that **old** **reading** **never** **existed**.  
- **Avoid retroactive erasure** of **prior** **understanding** — **errata** **tone** **over** **stealth** **rewrite**.  

---

### 6. Contradiction & multi-reading handling

- **Multiple valid interpretations** — **may** **coexist** in **commentary** space; **canon** **declares** **which** **claims** **bind** the **library**.  
- **Conflicting annotations** — **prefer** **threaded** **clarity** + **governance** **decision** over **silent** **delete**.  
- **Symbolic plurality** — **document** **scope** of each **reading**.  
- **Layered doctrine** — **meaning** vs **`doctrine`** vs **`underlay`** as **explicit** **layers** when used.  
- **Historical reinterpretation** — **new** **commentary** **explains** **shift**; **does not** **erase** **old** **without** **governed** **transition**.  

**Principles:** **Coexistence + annotation** preferred over **destructive** **flattening**. **Commentary may document disagreement** without **forcing** **false** **resolution** (**aligns** **CANON EVIDENCE** §5, **CANON TRANSITION** §6).

---

### 7. Traceability & context preservation

- **Preserve rationale / context** — **why** an **annotation** exists **links** to **review** or **audit**.  
- **Annotation traceability** — **authored** **attribution** (maintainer vs **Zierota** vs **tool**) when **meaningful**.  
- **Governance references** — cite **locks** / **pipelines** when **annotation** **touches** **tier** or **scope**.  
- **Historical commentary continuity** — **do not** **orphan** **old** **notes** **without** **redirect** narrative.  
- **Maintain distinction** — **UI** (**future**) **should** **visually** / **structurally** **separate** **canon** **body** from **commentary** **chrome**.  

---

### 8. Future implementation boundary

- **Future UI / tooling** may **render** annotations in **separate** bands, **sidebars**, or **modal** **layers** — **must** **preserve** **canon** **boundaries**.  
- **Commentary systems** must **not** **auto-merge** into **`doctrine`** or **`canon/`** without **ingestion** + **Zierota**.  
- **Automation** may **cluster**, **tag**, or **surface** commentary — **must not** **promote** it to **canon** or **raise** **confidence** **tiers** **alone**.  
- **Annotation governance** remains **platform-independent** — same rules for **Pages**, **Decap**, **static** **site**, or **future** **CMS**.  

---

### 9. Governance principles (explicit)

- **Commentary supplements rather than overrides canon.**  
- **Ambiguity may remain visible.**  
- **Interpretation is contextual.**  
- **Preserve historical readings** in **commentary** / **archive** **layers**.  
- **Avoid silent doctrinal inflation** — **no** **smuggling** **claims** via **notes**.  
- **Explanation ≠ declaration.**  
- **Annotation visibility ≠ authority.**  

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** canon **text** in **`sigils.json`** changed; **no** sigils **modified** by this lock.  
- **No** **commentary** system, **schema**, or **UI** implemented.  
- **No** **permissions**, **discoverability**, or **search** behavior changed.  
- **Governance definitions only** — **Cloudflare**, **PATH A**, **Decap/Identity** preserved; **lifecycle / transition / evidence** locks **unchanged** in **role**; this lock **adds annotation rules** only. **Companion** entity-relationship lock **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** graph or **`sigils.json`** relationship fields added). **Companion** meta-governance lock **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** governance tooling that amends locks). **Companion** consolidation/index lock **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** authority re-layering).

---

## CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **conceptual relationship semantics, association authority, and semantic-structure rules only.** **Builds on** **CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **CANON TRANSITION GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1**. **No** **`sigils.json`**, **schema**, **graph** or **database**, **relationship** fields, **search**/**discoverability**, **CMS**, **relationship UI**, deploy, package, or **automation** that **declares** doctrine from **edges** alone.

**Purpose:** Define how **relationships** between **sigils**, **doctrine**, **entities** (conceptual), **layers** (**meaning** / **`doctrine`** / **`underlay`** as **layers**, not a graph schema), **symbols**, **historical states**, **archive material**, and **interpretations** may be **represented and discussed** **without** **accidental** canon **authority** drift.

**Current reality preserved:** **Cloudflare** canonical deployment; **PATH A** Pages; **Decap/Identity** preserved; prior governance locks remain **conceptual** where stated; **no** relationship **graph** tooling exists; **no** canon transitions executed by this document. **Meta-governance** for how **locks** themselves **evolve** — **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**. **Constitutional index** for **cross-lock** reading order — **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1**.

---

### 1. Relationship taxonomy

Relationships are **contextual** — **not** all links imply **canon equality**; **not** all imply **causality** or **inheritance**.

| Relationship type | Typical meaning | Implies equality / causality? |
| ------------------- | ---------------- | ----------------------------- |
| **Direct doctrinal relationship** | **`canon/`**-stated or **ingested** **binding** claim between named entities | **Only** when **explicitly** **declared** |
| **Symbolic association** | Shared motif, geometry, color, **facet** echo | **No** — **heuristic** |
| **Historical lineage** | **Succession**, **fork**, **deprecation** chain, **reinterpretation** over **time** | **Temporal**, **not** automatic **equivalence** |
| **Interpretive linkage** | Reader/maintainer **reading** across entries | **No** — **annotation** tier (**CANON ANNOTATION**) |
| **Archive reference** | Pointer to **deprecated** / **archived** / **philosophy archive** material | **Context** for **memory**, **not** silent **current** **law** |
| **Structural dependency** | **Build**, routing, **slug** identity, **shared** **validator** surface | **System** truth — **distinct** from **lore** **declaration** |
| **Thematic resonance** | Register tone / **atmosphere** adjacency | **No** proof of **shared** **canon fact** |
| **Contradictory relationship** | **Tension** or **disclaim** between claims | **Documentary** — **governance** chooses **coexistence** vs **scope** |
| **Speculative linkage** | “**Might** relate” without **approved** text | **Lowest** **authority** |
| **Implementation / reference relationship** | Code ↔ **data** ↔ **media** **wiring** | **High** for **shipping** behavior; **low** for **new** **lore** |

---

### 2. Relationship authority levels

| Level | Meaning | Rules |
| ----- | ------- | ----- |
| **Declared doctrinal relationship** | **`canon/`** + **ingestion** **explicit** | **Highest** **lore** **link** authority |
| **Governance-confirmed linkage** | **Lock** or **PR** records **approved** **cross-reference** | **High** for **process**; **must** cite **canon** for **new** **binding** claims |
| **Historical association** | **Co-occurrence** in **time**, **shared** **checkpoint** | **Not** automatic **doctrine** |
| **Interpretive / symbolic association** | **Pattern** or **commentary** | **Contextual** — **CANON EVIDENCE** §1–§2 |
| **Speculative connection** | **Hypothesis** | **Must** stay **labeled** |
| **Unresolved linkage** | **Open** **tension** | **May** **persist** — **CANON ANNOTATION** / **EVIDENCE** |

**Clarifications:** **Visibility of a relationship ≠ authority.** **Symbolic resonance ≠ confirmed dependency.** **Repeated association ≠ canon proof** (**CANON EVIDENCE** stability epistemology).

---

### 3. Declared vs inferred relationships

| Kind | Definition | Rule |
| ---- | ---------- | ---- |
| **Explicitly declared** | **Written** in **approved** **`canon/`** and/or **ingested** **doctrine** with **clear** referential intent | **May** **bind** reader **contract** per **Zierota** |
| **Inferred** | **Derived** from **juxtaposition**, **tone**, or **sparse** hints | **Does not** automatically **become** doctrine |
| **Symbolic readings** | **Visual** / **lexical** **echo** | **Atmosphere** — **not** **standalone** proof |
| **Historical co-occurrence** | Same **era**, **same** **register** **work**, **shared** **audit** period | **Adjacency** **≠** **designed** **linkage** |
| **Speculative association** | **Undeclared** “**feels** related” | **Out of band** for **binding** **claims** |

**Inference does not automatically become doctrine.** **Historical adjacency is not automatic linkage.** **Interpretation may coexist with uncertainty** (**CANON ANNOTATION** §3).

---

### 4. Historical lineage governance

- **Historical evolution** — **annotate** **succession** (**deprecated → archived**, **reinterpretation**) rather than **erase** **prior** **readings**.  
- **Canon succession** — **new** **declared** **row** or **block** **explains** **relationship** to **predecessor**.  
- **Reinterpretation chains** — **stack** **governance** **notes**; **avoid** **retroactive** “**always** meant X.”  
- **Historical forks / abandoned branches** — **preserve** in **git** / **archive**; **optional** **pointers** in **commentary**.  
- **Preservation of prior meaning states** — **default** **retain** **evidence** of **old** **understanding**.  

**Lineage should preserve history rather than erase it.** **Newer interpretations do not silently destroy older ones.**

---

### 5. Contradiction & overlap governance

- **Conflicting relationship claims** — **document** **both**; **governance** picks **coexistence**, **scoped** **compatibility**, or **deprecation** — **CANON TRANSITION** §6.  
- **Overlapping symbolic systems** — **register** **clarity**; **avoid** **flattening** **distinct** **claims** into **one** **edge**.  
- **Competing lineage interpretations** — **may** **coexist** in **commentary**; **declared** **canon** **wins** for **binding** **library** **contract** only where **Zierota** **says** so.  
- **Semantic ambiguity** — **may** remain **visible**.  
- **Multi-layer meaning** — **explicit** **layer** (**meaning** vs **`doctrine`** vs **`underlay`**).  

**Coexistence + annotation preferred over flattening.** **Unresolved overlap may remain visible.**

---

### 6. Relationship confidence model

| Confidence | Meaning | Derives from |
| ---------- | ------- | ------------- |
| **Uncertain** | **Thin** basis | **Hypothesis** |
| **Speculative** | **Intentional** **maybe** | **Editorial** / **reader** **exploration** |
| **Interpretive** | **Pattern** reading | **Review** + **atmosphere** checks |
| **Historically supported** | **Git** / **archive** / **dated** **artifacts** | **Evidence** trail (**CANON EVIDENCE**) |
| **Reviewed** | **Cross-read** + **audit** | **Governance** **process** |
| **Stable** | **Long** **unchallenged** **declared** **link** | **Time** + **consistency** — **not** **popularity** alone |
| **Governance-confirmed** | **Lock** + **canon** **citation** | **Highest** for **new** **structural** **lore** **links** |

**Confidence derives from evidence + review + governance** — **not** from **repetition**, **routing**, or **graph** **layout** **prestige**.

---

### 7. Traceability & context preservation

- **Preserve relationship rationale** — **why** a **link** is **claimed** (**PR**, **lock**, **`reviewReference`** when used).  
- **Governance references** — cite **which** **lock** authorized **new** **binding** **cross-reference**.  
- **Historical context** — **date** or **phase** when **reading** **solidified** or **shifted**.  
- **Commentary separation** — **inferential** **edges** live in **annotation** / **masters**, **not** **smuggled** into **`doctrine`** **voice** **undeclared**.  
- **Relationship review notes** — **append** **when** **confidence** **changes**.  
- **Preserve ambiguity** where **honesty** requires — **CANON ANNOTATION** alignment.  

---

### 8. Future implementation boundary

- **Future UI / graph systems** may **visualize** relationships — **must** **encode** **authority** / **confidence** **visually** or **structurally** (**edge types**, **labels**, **filters**) per this lock.  
- **Relationship visualization must preserve authority distinctions** — **no** **default** “**all** **edges** **equal**.”  
- **Automation may surface associations** (co-mention, **n-gram**, **symbol** **overlap**) — **must not** **auto-declare** doctrine or **write** **`sigils.json`** **relationship** **claims** **without** **governance**.  
- **Governance rules remain platform-independent.**  

---

### 9. Governance principles (explicit)

- **Relationships supplement understanding rather than replace canon.**  
- **Association ≠ inheritance.**  
- **Resonance ≠ confirmation.**  
- **Visibility ≠ authority.**  
- **Preserve historical linkage context.**  
- **Avoid silent semantic inflation** via **undeclared** **edges** or **prose** **implication**.  
- **Maintain distinction between doctrine and interpretation.**  

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** relationships **implemented** in **data** or **code**; **no** **graph** system added.  
- **No** sigils **modified**; **no** **schema** or **discoverability**/**search** changes.  
- **No** **permissions** or **CMS** changes.  
- **Governance definitions only** — **Cloudflare**, **PATH A**, **Decap/Identity** preserved; **lifecycle / transition / evidence / annotation** locks **unchanged** in **role**; this lock **adds relationship semantics** only. **Companion** meta-governance lock **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** governance automation or autonomous lock edits). **Companion** consolidation/index lock **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**no** relationship **meaning** changes).

---

## GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **meta-governance: how governance systems and constitutional-style rules in masters may evolve without uncontrolled drift, silent authority escalation, or governance memory loss.** **Builds on** **DOCUMENTATION DISCIPLINE — LOCKED** (phase cadence in **`EMPYRRIA_MASTER.md`**), **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1**, **CANON TRANSITION GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, and **PATH A** editorial boundaries (**EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK**). **No** **`sigils.json`**, **no** canon text edits, **no** **schema**, **no** **CMS**/**admin**/**deploy**/**package** changes, **no** **permissions** or discoverability/search behavior changes, **no** **migrations** executed, **no** **governance automation** or bots that **amend** locks **autonomously**.

**Purpose:** Define **governance hierarchy**, **amendment authority**, **supersession** and **conflict** precedence, **stability tiers** for governance prose itself, **immutability vs evolvability**, **traceability** of governance change, and **governance archive** philosophy — so **operational** convenience cannot silently rewrite **constitutional** intent.

**Current reality preserved:** **Cloudflare Pages** canonical deployment; **PATH A** constrained **Pages CMS** active; **Decap**/**Identity** preserved; prior governance locks remain **conceptual** where stated; **no** governance automation exists; **no** canon transitions executed by this document.

**Constitutional navigation (companion lock):** **Read-order index**, **domain map**, and **terminology** guide across locks — **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1** (**does not** **change** **this** lock’s **meaning**).

---

### 1. Governance hierarchy model

**Not all governance text carries equal authority.** **Higher** layers **constrain** **lower** layers; **lower** layers **do not** **override** **higher** intent without a **traceable** amendment.

| Layer | Typical locus | Role | Subordination rule |
| ----- | ------------- | ---- | -------------------- |
| **Constitutional governance** | **`EMPYRRIA_MASTER.md`** + **CODEX** **authoritative roots** (**AUTHORITATIVE POLICY ROOTS**), core **non-goals** / **identity** guardrails | **Stability** of **project meaning**, **archive** posture, **anti-drift** spine | **Supersedes** **operational** shortcuts; **amend** only via **explicit** governance change (**this lock** + **locks**/**PR** trail) |
| **Canon governance** | **`canon/`**, **ingestion pipeline**, **Zierota** approval, **`sigils.json`** policy in masters | **What** counts as **Empyrria** library canon | **Subordinate** to **Zierota**; **masters** describe **process**, **not** invent **lore** |
| **Editorial governance** | **PATH A**, **Decap**/**Identity** role texts, enrichment **RFCs**, **controlled** editorial passes | **How** approved text **matures** within **bounds** | **Cannot** silently **redefine** **constitutional** or **canon** tiers |
| **Infrastructure governance** | **Hosting**, **branch**, **build**, **validators**, **routes**, **legacy** inventory locks | **Ship** and **rollback** truth | **High** for **system behavior**; **does not** **grant** new **lore** or **canon** **tier** moves **without** **canon** path |
| **Implementation governance** | **Layout**/**Phase A** plans, **component** conventions, **data** wiring docs | **Execution** detail | **Subordinate** to **governance intent** — **code** **implements**, **does not** **reinterpret** **constitutional** rules |
| **Operational guidance** | **“Current next step”**, **checklists**, **warnings** in masters | **Day-to-day** steering | **Lowest** **binding** **weight** — **may** **lag** reality; **must not** **contradict** active **LOCK** **scope** **undeclared** |
| **Commentary / reference material** | **Cross-links**, **audit** narratives, **philosophy archive** pointers | **Context** and **memory** | **Non-authoritative** for **new** **binding** claims unless **promoted** via **canon** or **lock** path |

**Clarifications:** **Constitutional layers supersede operational convenience.** **Implementation layers remain subordinate to governance intent.** **Visibility** of a paragraph (length, position) **≠** **constitutional** authority.

---

### 2. Amendment authority model

| Action | Definition | Typical requirement |
| ------ | ---------- | --------------------- |
| **Clarification** | **Wording** that **restates** or **disambiguates** **unchanged** intent (**typos**, **scannability**, **cross-links**) | **Light** review — **still** **git**-visible; **must not** **smuggle** new **obligations** |
| **Amendment** | **Material** change to **obligations**, **scope**, **non-goals**, **authority** splits, or **supersession** of a **prior** rule | **Formal** **lock** update or **new** **lock** + **CODEX** table row + **rationale** (**PR** / **commit** body) |
| **Operational drift repair** | Fix **stale** “next step” or **broken** links **without** changing **rules** | **Editorial** — **label** as **non-amendment** when **ambiguous** |
| **Escalation / review** | Any change that **could** **raise** **PATH A**, **tier**, **infra**, or **canon** **authority** | **CANON TRANSITION** escalation mindset — **governance** **first** |

**Who / what may amend governance:** **Maintainers** draft; **project** practice treats **merged** **lock** text and **MASTER**/**CODEX** **agreement** as **binding** for **phase** scope. **Zierota** remains **ultimate** **canon** authority for **lore**; **masters** **do not** replace **Zierota** for **declarations**.

**Rules:** **Convenience does not justify constitutional drift.** **Silent amendment is prohibited** — if **readers** would **reasonably** infer a **new** **duty** or **permission**, the change is an **amendment**, **not** a **clarification**, and **must** be **labeled** and **traceable**. **What requires formal governance locks:** **codex-wide** rule changes, **authority** redistribution, **execution** of retirement/migration, **CMS**/**schema**/**discoverability** policy shifts — align with **CANON TRANSITION** **L3–L5** spirit. **What may evolve operationally:** **stale** pointers, **non-normative** examples, **checklist** hygiene — **without** changing **LOCK** **meaning**.

---

### 3. Governance stability tiers

| Tier | Meaning | Change friction |
| ---- | ------- | ----------------- |
| **Exploratory governance** | **RFC**/**draft** language, **hypothesis** sections | **Low** — **must** be **labeled** **non-locked** |
| **Provisional governance** | **Phase 1** vocabulary and **process** definitions **awaiting** practice stress-test | **Moderate** — **prefer** **additive** **narrowing** over **silent** **broadening** |
| **Stable governance** | **LOCKED** sections that have **proven** **operational** without **contradiction** **surprises** | **Higher** — **amend** with **explicit** **supersession** note |
| **Constitutional governance** | **Identity**, **archive philosophy**, **authoritative roots**, **non-goals** that **define** **what the project is** | **Highest** — **resist** **casual** change; **amend** only with **strong** **rationale** + **continuity** language |
| **Deprecated governance** | **Superseded** rule blocks **kept** for **memory** | **Frozen** — **edit** only for **link** rot / **danger** **misreads** |
| **Historical governance artifact** | **Philosophy archive**, **checkpoint** narratives, **superseded** master bodies | **Append**/**annotate**; **do not** **pretend** **past** **locks** **never** **existed** |

**Stronger tiers resist casual change.** **Governance history should remain preserved** in **git**, **archive** files, and **explicit** **supersession** lines.

---

### 4. Supersession & conflict rules

- **Conflicting governance statements** — **do not** **flatten** by **deleting** the **older** text **without** **trace**; **prefer** **supersession** header (**“Supersedes …”** / **“Narrowed by …”**) + **date** + **lock** id.  
- **Superseded rules** — **remain** **legible** in **history** or **deprecated** blocks; **new** rule **states** **what** **changes** for **operators**.  
- **Overlapping governance phases** — **name** the **active** lock for **scope**; **later** **Phase 1** docs **clarify** they **add** **slices**, **not** **erase** **prior** **locks** **unless** **explicit**.  
- **Contradictory operational guidance** — if **“next step”** **fights** a **LOCK**, **fix** **operational** text **or** **re-open** governance **deliberately** — **not** **silent** **winner**.  
- **Amendment precedence** — **later explicit amendment** **wins** over **earlier** text **only** **within** the **scope** **declared**; **out-of-scope** **implied** **repeal** is **invalid**.  

**Newer governance does not silently erase historical governance.** **Supersession should remain traceable.** **Contradictions require annotation or escalation** — align with **CANON ANNOTATION** and **CANON ENTITY** tension-handling spirit.

---

### 5. Governance traceability

- **Preserve rationale** — **PR** description, **lock** **Purpose**/**Strict boundary**, **commit** message when **material**.  
- **Amendment references** — **cite** **supersedes** / **narrows** / **clarifies** **which** **section** or **lock**.  
- **Governance lineage** — **readers** should see **evolution** (**why** **this** **rule** **exists** **now**).  
- **Lock references** — **new** **work** that **contradicts** an **old** **lock** **must** **name** the **lock** it **replaces** or **narrows**.  
- **Historical governance context** — **checkpoint** ids, **`EMPYRRIA_PHILOSOPHY_ARCHIVE.md`**, **dated** **status** lines.  
- **Preserving why governance changed** — **avoid** **“because we felt like it”** as **sole** **justification** for **constitutional** edits.  

---

### 6. Immutability vs evolvability

| Category | Intent | May evolve? |
| -------- | ------ | ----------- |
| **Foundational principles** | **Doctrine-first**, **atmosphere**, **sparse validity**, **Zierota** **ownership** of **lore** | **Very slowly** — **label** **philosophy** **shift** if **real** |
| **Amendable operational procedures** | **Ingestion** order, **build** gate, **escalation** ladder **details** | **Yes** — with **locks**/**PR** when **material** |
| **Experimental governance ideas** | **RFCs**, **deferred** Phase **B** | **Yes** — **must** stay **non-binding** until **locked** |
| **Temporary guidance** | **Pause** windows, **observation-only** posture | **Yes** — **expiry** or **successor** lock **should** **state** **what** **replaces** it |
| **Implementation-specific rules** | **Tailwind**/**Astro**/**CMS** wiring **notes** | **Yes** — **must not** **reinterpret** **canon** or **constitutional** **authority** |

**Some principles intentionally resist change.** **Implementation may evolve while principles remain stable.**

---

### 7. Governance archive philosophy

- **Deprecated governance preservation** — **keep** **superseded** paragraphs or **move** to **archive** with **pointer**, **not** **orphan** **history**.  
- **Historical governance artifacts** — **philosophy archive**, **tags**, **long** **checkpoints** are **first-class** **memory**.  
- **Governance archaeology** — **future** readers may **need** **why** a **strange** **rule** **once** **made sense**.  
- **Preserving prior constitutional reasoning** — **quote** or **summarize** **old** **core** **argument** when **narrowing**.  
- **Avoiding governance memory loss** — **no** **force-push** **rewrite** of **governance** **history** for **aesthetics**.  

---

### 8. Future implementation boundary

- **Future tooling** may **assist** governance **navigation** (indexes, **diff** views, **“active locks”** dashboards) — **human** **readers** remain **accountable** for **interpretation**.  
- **Automation must not autonomously amend governance** — **CI** may **flag** **stale**/**contradictory** docs; **cannot** **merge** **lock** **text** **without** **human** **intent**.  
- **Governance authority remains human / constitutional** — **bots**, **LLMs**, and **scaffolds** **do not** **ratify** **amendments**.  
- **Governance model remains platform-independent** — **same** **meta-rules** if **Pages**, **Decap**, or **plain git** **dominates** editing.  

---

### 9. Governance principles (explicit)

- **Governance before convenience.**  
- **Preserve constitutional continuity.**  
- **Avoid silent authority drift.**  
- **Trace supersession explicitly.**  
- **Preserve governance history.**  
- **Implementation does not override intent.**  
- **Clarification ≠ amendment.**  
- **Visibility ≠ constitutional authority.**  

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** governance **permissions** changed; **no** **systems** removed; **no** canon or **`sigils.json`** modified.  
- **No** runtime behavior, **schema**, **CMS**, **deploy**, **package**, **discoverability**, or **migration** **execution** from this lock.  
- **No** **governance automation** introduced.  
- **Governance definitions only** — **Cloudflare**, **PATH A**, **Decap/Identity** preserved; **lifecycle / transition / evidence / annotation / entity-relationship** locks **unchanged** in **role**; this lock **adds meta-governance** only. **Companion** consolidation/index lock **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1** is **also** documentation-only (**navigation** and **mapping** only — **no** **amendment** of **prior** **lock** **text** **by reference** alone).

---

## GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **constitutional navigation and consolidation index only.** **Does not** alter **meaning**, **authority**, or **obligations** of **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1**, **CANON TRANSITION GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **CANON ENTITY RELATIONSHIP GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**, **AUTHORITATIVE POLICY ROOTS**, **PATH A** locks, or **canon**/**implementation** locks. **No** **`sigils.json`**, **no** canon edits, **no** schema, **no** CMS/deploy/package/discoverability/runtime changes, **no** migrations, **no** automation. **Substantive** rules remain **only** in their **home** sections; **this lock** adds **index**, **maps**, and **terminology guidance** only.

**Purpose:** Make **where** authoritative definitions live, **how** governance **domains** connect, and **which** concepts **depend** on **which** — **readability** and **overlap awareness**, **not** redesign.

**Current reality preserved:** **Cloudflare Pages** canonical deployment; **PATH A** constrained **Pages CMS** active; **Decap**/**Identity** preserved; existing domain locks remain **authoritative**; **no** governance automation.

---

### 1. Constitutional index model

**Domains** (each has a **home lock** or **root** — **cited** for **binding** text):

| Governance domain | Authoritative home (read **there** for **rules**) | Companion / cross-links |
| ------------------- | -------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------- |
| **Lifecycle + stability vocabulary** | **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1** | **CANON TRANSITION** (moves); **CANON INGESTION PIPELINE — LOCKED** (entry) |

| **Evidence + review epistemology** | **CANON EVIDENCE & REVIEW GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** | **CONTENT**; **CANON TRANSITION**; **CANON ANNOTATION** |
| **Annotation + commentary boundaries** | **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1** | **CANON EVIDENCE**; **CANON ENTITY** (edges vs doctrine) |

| **Archive + deprecation philosophy (content)** | **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1** (archive bands) + **`EMPYRRIA_PHILOSOPHY_ARCHIVE.md`** | **CANON TRANSITION**; **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** |
| **Operational + editorial (tooling)** | **EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK** (**PATH A**); **ZIEROTA ADMIN ACCESS — PHASE 1**; **ZIEROTA EDITORIAL PRESSURE LOG — PHASE 1**; **TEXT RENDERING & DISPLAY ERGONOMICS — PHASE 1**; **EDITORIAL FIELD EVOLUTION — PHASE 1**; **PATH A GOVERNANCE FIELD HIDING — PHASE 1**; **PAGES CMS VALIDATION AUDIT — LOCK**; **POST-MIGRATION LEGACY SYSTEM AUDIT — LOCK** | **CONTENT**; **CANON TRANSITION**; **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE** (pressure observation) |
| **Doctrine / atmosphere roots** | **AUTHORITATIVE POLICY ROOTS — STABLE** (CODEX) | Editorial execution RFCs and audits |
| **Stabilization + observational window** | **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW** | **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION**; all domain locks; **CONTENT** review triggers; **ZIEROTA EDITORIAL PRESSURE LOG — PHASE 1** (classified PATH A friction) |
| **Full entry prototype (planning)** | **FULL ENTRY PROTOTYPE — PHASE 1** | **CANON ANNOTATION**; **CANON ENTITY**; **CANON EVIDENCE**; **TOP-IRON-ENDURANCE PHASE A IMPLEMENTATION** (live specimen); **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE** |
| **Full entry visual mockup (planning)** | **FULL ENTRY VISUAL MOCKUP — PHASE 1** | **FULL ENTRY PROTOTYPE — PHASE 1**; **CANON ANNOTATION**; **CANON ENTITY**; **AUTHORITATIVE POLICY ROOTS** (doctrine-first, atmosphere protection); **TOP-IRON-ENDURANCE PHASE A IMPLEMENTATION** (live reference); **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE** |
| **Specimen entry wireframe (planning)** | **SPECIMEN ENTRY WIREFRAME — PHASE 1** | **FULL ENTRY PROTOTYPE — PHASE 1**; **FULL ENTRY VISUAL MOCKUP — PHASE 1** (structure vs aesthetics); **CANON ANNOTATION**; **CANON ENTITY**; **CANON EVIDENCE**; **AUTHORITATIVE POLICY ROOTS** (doctrine-first, sparse density); **TOP-IRON-ENDURANCE PHASE A IMPLEMENTATION** (structural reference); **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE** |

**Operational vs constitutional:** **“Current next step”** paragraphs are **steering**, **not** a **second** constitution. **LOCKED** phase sections and **authoritative roots** carry **rule** weight.

---

### 2. Source-of-truth hierarchy

| Layer | **`EMPYRRIA_MASTER.md`** | **`EMPYRRIA_CODEX_MASTER.md`** |
| ----- | ------------------------ | ------------------------------ |
| **Policies, checkpoints summary, discipline headline, condensed governance rules** | **Primary** readable entry for **operators** | **Authoritative** for **full** lock text, tables, and **implementation map** |
| **Conflict between MASTER and CODEX on facts** | Per **MASTER** rule: align **before** continuing | **CODEX** usually **wins** on **depth**; **MASTER** must **not** **drift** on **URLs**, **dates**, **counts** **undeclared** |

**Governance definition ownership:** **Domain locks** own their **definitions**; **this index** owns **cross-reference topology** only. **Implementation references** (file paths, commands) in **CODEX** are **high authority for “what ships”** but **do not** override **Zierota** **canon** or **lock** **scope**. **Avoid duplicated constitutional authority** — do **not** re-state full matrices in **MASTER** when **CODEX** is **canonical** for that lock.

---

### 3. Governance domain map (dependencies)

**Dependencies are conceptual** — **read order** for clarity, **not** a runtime call graph.

| From (consumer) | Depends on (supplier concept) | Interaction boundary |
| ----------------- | ----------------------------- | ---------------------- |
| **CANON TRANSITION** | **CONTENT** (lifecycle language) | Transition lock **does not** redefine states |
| **CANON EVIDENCE** | **CONTENT**; **CANON TRANSITION** | Epistemology **does not** execute transitions |
| **CANON ANNOTATION** | **CANON EVIDENCE**; **CONTENT**; **CANON TRANSITION** | Commentary **does not** **promote** doctrine |
| **CANON ENTITY** | **CANON EVIDENCE**; **CANON ANNOTATION**; **CANON TRANSITION** | Links **do not** equal doctrine |
| **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** | **All** domain locks; **DOCUMENTATION DISCIPLINE** | Meta rules **constrain** **how** text may **change** |
| **This index** | **All** of the above | **Navigation only** |

**Overlapping concerns:** **“Authority”** appears in **CONTENT**, **EVIDENCE**, **ENTITY**, **ANNOTATION**, **EVOLUTION** — same **word**, **layer-specific** nuance; **do not** assume **one paragraph** **imports** another lock’s **full** meaning.

---

### 4. Terminology normalization (preferred readings)

Use **these** senses in **governance prose** unless a **lock** **explicitly** narrows further:

| Term | Preferred constitutional meaning |
| ---- | -------------------------------- |
| **Canon** | **Zierota-approved** material carried through **`canon/`** + **ingestion** into **public** library contract |
| **Commentary / annotation** | Speech **around** canon — **CANON ANNOTATION** taxonomy |
| **Authority** | **Who/what may bind** operators or readers — **layer-specific** (process vs lore vs tooling) |
| **Governance** | **Documented rules and locks** — **not** informal habit |
| **Lifecycle** | **CONTENT** state **vocabulary** — **not** automatically equal to single JSON keys |
| **Stability** | **Tier expectations** for change friction — **CONTENT** + **CANON TRANSITION** |
| **Evidence** | **Graded justification** for claims — **CANON EVIDENCE** |
| **Interpretation vs declaration** | **Derived reading** vs **explicit binding** — **CANON EVIDENCE** / **CANON ANNOTATION** |
| **Relationship (sigil/doctrine)** | **Conceptual link** with **typed** authority — **CANON ENTITY** |
| **Archive** | **Preserved posture** — material **legible** but **disclaimed** or **non-primary** where policy says |
| **Supersession** | **Traceable** replacement or narrowing of governance or doctrine text — **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** |

**Preserve contextual nuance** where a lock **already** defines a narrower sense; **this table** is a **default coordination** layer.

---

### 5. Redundancy & overlap governance

- **Intentional overlap** — repeated anchors (**governance before convenience**, **visibility ≠ authority**) **reinforce** stability; **treat** as **echo**, **not** **new law** each time.  
- **Companion locks** — **CONTENT** ↔ **TRANSITION** ↔ **EVIDENCE** ↔ **ANNOTATION** ↔ **ENTITY** ↔ **EVOLUTION**; **this index** lists **companions**, **does not** **merge** them into **one** **super-lock**.  
- **Accidental duplication** — same **matrix** pasted in **two** places **without** pointing to **authoritative** home risks **fork**; **prefer** **link** + **short summary**.  
- **Duplication must not create conflicting authority** — if **two** blocks **disagree**, **neither** **this index** nor **operational** blurbs **decide**; **escalate** per **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** and **fix** **domain** text.  

---

### 6. Governance dependency model (conceptual stack)

**Foundational downward pressure** (upper constrains lower): **Authoritative roots** and **constitutional posture** → **meta-governance** (**GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION**) → **domain locks** (**CONTENT** … **ENTITY**) → **operational guidance**. **Lower layers must not override foundational layers** without **traceable amendment**. **`EMPYRRIA_PHILOSOPHY_ARCHIVE.md`** preserves **historical governance genealogy**; **does not** override **current** **LOCK** scope.

---

### 7. Constitutional navigation principles

- **Constitutional clarity over convenience** — prefer **one authoritative home** + **links**.  
- **Preserve authoritative source boundaries** — index **maps**, **does not** **vacuum** text upward.  
- **Avoid hidden governance forks** — if **two** versions exist, **name** **which** is **active** for **scope**.  
- **Maintain cross-reference traceability** — tables here **point**, **domain locks** **bind**.  
- **Preserve governance readability as the codex grows** — append **index rows**, **avoid** **giant** merged slabs.  
- **Navigation does not alter authority** — **reordering** paragraphs in a **future** **presentation** refactor **does not** itself **amend** locks (**GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION**).  

---

### 8. Future consolidation boundary

- **Future refactors** may **reorganize** governance **presentation** (TOC, splits) — **must** preserve **meaning** and **git**/**supersession** history.  
- **Restructuring does not imply supersession** — **file move** ≠ **new rule** unless **locks** say so.  
- **Tooling / navigation layers** (indexes, sidebars) **remain subordinate** to **constitutional** and **domain** authority.  

---

### 9. Governance traceability (for this index)

- **Lock lineage** — when **adding** a **row** to **Locked implementation progress**, keep **date** + **scope** consistent.  
- **Governance ancestry** — **philosophy archive** + **checkpoints** stay **linked** from **MASTER** / **CODEX** **where** relevant.  
- **Companion integrity** — domain lock **companion** bullets **should** stay **mutually consistent** with **this map**.  
- **Cross-reference integrity** — broken **anchor** text fixed as **editorial** repair; **not** silent **reinterpretation**.  
- **Historical context during consolidation** — when **collating**, **retain** **dates** and **supersedes** notes per **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION**.  

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** governance **authority** changed; **no** **constitutional** **meaning** changed; **no** canon or **`sigils.json`** modified.  
- **No** systems removed; **no** runtime, discoverability, **CMS**, deploy, package, schema, migration, or automation changes.  
- **Consolidation and constitutional navigation definitions only** — **Cloudflare**, **PATH A**, **Decap/Identity** preserved; **all** cited domain locks **unchanged** in **binding role**.  

---

## SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **stabilization and observational governance only.** Intentional **pause on major constitutional / governance-stack expansion** (unnecessary new governance domains, speculative phase locks, broad ontology or schema hardening, **premature** automation governance) so the **existing** stack (**CONTENT**, **CANON TRANSITION**, **CANON EVIDENCE**, **CANON ANNOTATION**, **CANON ENTITY**, **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION**, **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION**, archive/traceability philosophy, **PATH A**) can **settle** under **real** operational use. **Does not** forbid **Zierota-approved** **canon** work, **CANON INGESTION** pipeline additions, **PATH A** / **Decap** editorial activity, **content growth**, **archive** maintenance, **implementation planning**, or **tooling research** — those **continue** per **existing** locks. **No** **`sigils.json`** or runtime change **implied by this document alone**; **no** new **binding** obligations beyond **prior** locks.

**Purpose:** Prevent **governance overgrowth** and **conceptual churn**; **prioritize operational validation**; let **organic friction** surface; **treat stability** as an **active governance objective**.

**Current reality preserved:** **Cloudflare Pages** canonical deployment; **PATH A** constrained **Pages CMS**; **Decap**/**Identity** preserved; domain locks remain **authoritative**; **no** governance automation; **no** canon transitions **executed by this lock**.

**Authoritative maturation-pause philosophy, observational stability window, allowed/discouraged activity, pressure-detection model, governance health principles, future resumption, traceability and observation notes, implementation boundary, and no-behavior-change:** this section. **Cross-index:** **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1**.

---

### 1. Maturation pause philosophy

- **Avoid constitutional overgrowth** — the stack is **adequate** for present **operation**; **resist** new layers for **theoretical completeness** alone.  
- **Prevent unnecessary abstraction** — **ontology** / **typed** governance **expansion** waits for **demonstrated** pressure, not **speculation**.  
- **Prioritize operational validation** — **ship**, **edit**, **read**, **notice** where stewards and readers **actually** struggle.  
- **Allow real-world friction to emerge naturally** — avoid **pre-emptive** bureaucracy that **masks** real bottlenecks.  
- **Theoretical vs operational needs** — **paper** elegance **≠** proven **pain**; new governance follows **demonstrated** need (**GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION & AMENDMENT GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**).  

**Authority references:** **ATMOSPHERE PROTECTION — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**, **SPARSE ENTRY + DENSITY GOVERNANCE — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**, **COMPATIBILITY-FIRST EVOLUTION — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**, **SELECTIVE ENRICHMENT GOVERNANCE — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**.

---

### 2. Observational stability window

**Purpose of observation:** use a **deliberate window** to watch whether **existing** governance is **usable**, **legible**, and **stable** under **actual** codex use.

**Observe (non-exhaustive):**

- **Governance usability** — can maintainers find the **right** lock? (**GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION & CONSTITUTIONAL INDEX — PHASE 1**)  
- **Editorial clarity** — **PATH A** vs **Decap**/**Identity** paths **coherent** for editors?  
- **Canon stability** — unintended **register** / tone drift; **doctrine** tension across sigils (**CONTENT** / audits)  
- **Terminology drift** — same word, **layer-inconsistent** senses across sections  
- **Redundancy pressure** — helpful **constitutional echo** vs **fork** risk  
- **Missing governance areas** — recurring questions **no** lock **answers**  
- **Operational bottlenecks** — **build**, **ingest**, **review**, **CMS** friction patterns  
- **Register / atmosphere signals** — register drift; phrase repetition escalation; overlap pressure; atmosphere fatigue; cadence predictability; accidental genre drift; unnecessary density growth; symbolic flattening  

**Clarifications:** **Absence of immediate new locks is intentional** — it is **not** proof the codex is “finished,” but that **stability** is **actively chosen**. **Stability itself is a governance objective.** Observation **does not** mandate immediate intervention.

---

### 3. Allowed during stability window

**Continues normally** when consistent with **existing** locks:

- **Content growth** and **canon work** — **approved** **`canon/`** + **CANON INGESTION PIPELINE — LOCKED** + **`npm run build`** gate  
- **Annotations / commentary** — per **CANON ANNOTATION & COMMENTARY GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**  
- **Operational editorial work** — **PATH A** fields; **Decap** + **Identity** **higher-authority** paths per **EDITORIAL SCOPE DECISION — LOCK**  
- **Archive work** — **philosophy archive**, checkpoints, **deprecated** / **archived** posture per **CONTENT GOVERNANCE MATURITY — PHASE 1** / **CANON TRANSITION GOVERNANCE — PHASE 1**  
- **Implementation planning** — RFCs **documented** as **non-binding** until **execution** locks  
- **Tooling research** — spikes **must not** silently amend governance (**§9**)  
- **Governance clarification** — **typo**, **link**, **scannability**, **cross-reference** fixes that **do not** amend obligations (**GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION**: clarification ≠ amendment)  

**Current stable state (supports observation):** coherent doctrinal registers; stable archive voice; sustainable lightweight architecture; acceptable symbolic repetition levels; successful sparse/dense coexistence; healthy dossier layering. **No immediate architectural pressure is currently required** for **new** **system** layers.

---

### 4. Discouraged during stability window

**Generally slow down** unless **demonstrated pressure** (**§5**) justifies a **new** lock (**§7**):

- **Unnecessary new constitutional layers** — new governance **domains** without a **pressure record**  
- **Speculative governance expansion** — “**might need someday**” **locks**  
- **Duplicate governance domains** — overlapping matrices **without** an **indexed** authoritative home (**GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION**)  
- **Premature automation governance** — **CI** / **bots** **authoring** or **reinterpreting** locks  
- **Over-abstracted ontology growth** — forced **typed** semantics before **documented** **semantic pressure** (defer per **UNIVERSAL SIGIL DOSSIER ARCHITECTURE RFC** posture)  
- **Governance for hypothetical systems** — rules for features **not** on a **shipped** or **locked** path  

**Anti-reaction discipline:** do **not** respond to **early** noise by forcing **ontology** systems, introducing **decorative** prose sprawl, **over-diversifying** vocabulary, adding **architecture** complexity, **inflating** lore density, or creating **semantic** bureaucracy. Evolve only when pressure is **sustained** and **structurally** meaningful.

---

### 5. Governance pressure detection

Signals that **may** justify **future** governance expansion (require **evidence**, **not** single anecdotes):

- **Recurring ambiguity** — the same governance question **reopens** across **PRs** or sessions  
- **Unresolved authority collisions** — **PATH A** vs **canon** vs **infra** **conflicts** **linger** after **good-faith** resolution attempts  
- **Repeated operational friction** — **build**, **ingest**, or **editorial** **breakage** **patterns**  
- **Traceability failures** — cannot reconstruct **why** a rule or **tier** changed  
- **Editorial confusion** — **misapplication** of **visibility** / **authority** splits  
- **Canon instability** — **reader-contract** shifts **without** **ingestion** / **lock** discipline  
- **Annotation leakage** — commentary **voice** **bleeding** into **doctrine** (**CANON ANNOTATION**)  
- **Relationship ambiguity** — **edge** pressure **without** **CANON ENTITY** clarity  
- **Implementation pressure** — **shipping** **blocked** **only** by **missing** governance **clarity** (still needs **human** **ratified** text, **not** code **alone**)  

**Rule:** **Governance grows from demonstrated need**, **not** speculative completeness.

---

### 6. Governance health principles

- **Stability is valuable** — fewer rule oscillations **reduce** hidden drift.  
- **Readability matters** — **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION** navigability is part of **health**.  
- **Constitutional restraint prevents drift** — pause **blocks** **reactive** layer sprawl.  
- **Governance should remain navigable** — prefer **index + links** over **multiplying** duplicate slabs.  
- **Operational reality informs future refinement** — observe first, **then** **lock**.  
- **Fewer stronger principles** over **excessive fragmentation** — align with **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** hierarchy.  

**Maturity posture:** Empyrria behaves as a **governed symbolic archive**. Growth priority: **calibration**, **restraint**, **doctrinal clarity**, **semantic integrity** — over **quantity**, **density**, **complexity**.

---

### 7. Future governance resumption

- **Future governance expansion remains possible** — the pause is **strategic**, **not** permanent.  
- **New locks** require **demonstrated pressure** (**§5**) or **clear** steward / **Zierota** value with **PR** / **rationale** (**GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION**).  
- **Integrate with the constitutional index** — update **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION** domain map; **avoid** orphan phases.  
- **Preserve continuity** — **supersede** or **narrow** **explicitly**; **avoid** unnecessary **forks**.  

**Reentry (material triggers — non-exhaustive):** a sigil **genuinely** needs refinement; **semantic** pressure **accumulates**; **overlap** drift **repeats**; **canon expansion** **justifies** added governance **burden**; **visual–doctrine** pressure emerges; dossier limits become **materially** constraining; **or** sustained signals from **§5**.

---

### 8. Traceability & observation

- **Record meaningful pressure points** — **PR** threads, **LIVE EXPERIENCE OBSERVATION PASS** / **LIGHTWEIGHT OBSERVATION LOG TEMPLATE PASS** where used, steward notes (**non-binding** unless **promoted** via locks)  
- **Preserve operational observations** — **dated** entries; **link** to relevant **locks**  
- **Identify recurring governance tensions** — distinguish **themes** from **one-off** incidents  
- **Isolated incidents vs systemic gaps** — a single typo ≠ a new domain; **pattern** + **impact** **matter**  

---

### 9. Future implementation boundary

- **Implementation may continue independently** — routes, **UI**, **validators**, **spikes**, per **COMPATIBILITY-FIRST EVOLUTION** and **separate** execution locks.  
- **Governance pause does not block operational or tooling evolution** — **shipping** is **not** forbidden; **silent** implied **governance** change **is** forbidden.  
- **Implementation remains subordinate to constitutional governance** — code **does not** **reinterpret** **canon** or **tier** authority.  
- **Tooling experimentation does not implicitly amend governance** — experiments **must not** **declare** new **obligations** without **human-ratified** lock text (**GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** future-implementation boundary by analogy).  

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** governance **authority** changed; **no** **constitutional** meaning of prior locks **changed by this section**.  
- **No** canon modified **by this lock**; **no** lifecycle **data** changes **from this lock**; **no** systems removed.  
- **No** runtime, **schema**, **CMS**, deploy, package, discoverability, migration execution, or automation introduced **here**.  
- **Stabilization and observational governance definitions only** — **Cloudflare**, **PATH A**, **Decap/Identity** preserved; existing locks **unchanged** in **binding role**.  

---

## SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW — LOCK / RESULT

**Status:** **LOCKED** — stabilization window documented and active as governance intent.

### Result record

- Established **maturation pause** on **major constitutional / governance-stack expansion** while **canon**, **content**, and **PATH A** work **continue** per **existing** locks.  
- Confirmed **observational stability window** intent: **usability**, **legibility**, **stability**, **pressure detection** (**§1–§10**).  
- Documented **allowed vs discouraged** activity, **health principles**, **implementation boundary**, and **no-behavior-change** guardrails.  
- Preserved **trigger-based** reentry and **GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION** cross-index alignment for **future** resumption.  

### Future caution notes

- Do not confuse temporary phrase overlap with systemic failure.
- Do not reopen maturation solely for momentum.
- Reentry should be trigger-based, not schedule-based.

---

## FULL ENTRY PROTOTYPE — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **documentation and planning only:** conceptual structure for **one** canonical **specimen** full codex entry as a **governance bridge** to future presentation—**not** system-wide architecture, **not** automation, **not** schema migration, **not** mass rollout. **No** **`sigils.json`** edits **by this lock**, **no** routes/components, **no** graph engine, **no** relationship **data**, **no** discoverability or CMS changes, **no** deploy/package work.

**Purpose:** **Pressure-test** constitutional layering (**CANON ANNOTATION**, **CANON ENTITY**, **CANON EVIDENCE**, **CONTENT**, **CANON TRANSITION**) through **readability** and **authority-separation** thinking; **observe** practical layering and **organic** friction; **bridge** philosophy into **future** UI/data design **without** amending governance **meaning**.

**Relationship to shipped work:** **`TOP-IRON-ENDURANCE PHASE A IMPLEMENTATION`** remains the **live** Phase **A** specimen; **this lock** names **how** a **fully realized** entry **could** be **read** and **layered** in principle—**observational** and **prototype-oriented**, **subordinate** to all domain locks.

**Current reality preserved:** **Cloudflare Pages** canonical; **PATH A** Pages CMS; **Decap**/**Identity** preserved; constitutional stack **unchanged** in **authority**; **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW** remains **active**; **no** graph tooling; **no** canon transitions **executed here**.

---

### 1. Prototype purpose

- **Pressure-test constitutional layering** — see whether **concepts** survive **one** dense reading surface.  
- **Validate readability** — ceremony vs **clarity** (**ATMOSPHERE PROTECTION**).  
- **Validate canon / commentary separation** — **CANON ANNOTATION** boundaries in **presentation** terms only.  
- **Observe annotation density** — risk of **overload** vs **honest** uncertainty.  
- **Observe relationship visibility** — **CANON ENTITY** confidence/authority in **layout** sketches **only** (no edges in data).  
- **Test authority signaling** — labels, tone, placement (**visibility ≠ authority**).  
- **Test historical layering** — archive / deprecated / reinterpretation **read order**.  
- **Test traceability presentation** — locks, **PR** refs, **reviewReference** without **dominating** the page.  

**Clarifications:** The **prototype is observational**; it **does not redefine** governance. **Prototype does not imply system-wide rollout**—each future surface needs its **own** execution lock.

---

### 2. Specimen entry layer model (conceptual)

| Layer | Typical content (conceptual) | Authority note |
| ----- | ----------------------------- | -------------- |
| **Canon body** | **`doctrine`**, identity **`meaning`**, approved **`canon/`** voice | **Highest** lore binding per **ingestion** |
| **Commentary / annotation layer** | Notes, **interpretive** gloss, **uncertainty** | **Subordinate** — **CANON ANNOTATION** |
| **Evidence / review layer** | **`reviewReference`**, audit pointers, **why** confidence | **Process** weight — **CANON EVIDENCE** |
| **Relationship layer** | Related sigils, **typed** links, **confidence** labels | **Semantic** only in planning—**CANON ENTITY** |
| **Historical / archive layer** | Deprecated readings, **archive** pointers | **Context** — **CONTENT** archive philosophy |
| **Governance references** | “**Governed by** …” pointers to **locks** | **Meta** — **does not** add new lore |
| **Traceability layer** | **PR**, **version**, **checkpoint** ids | **Memory** for maintainers |
| **Implementation notes** | Build/CMS **behavior** | **System** truth — **distinct** from canon |
| **Authority / stability indicators** | **Provisional**, **stable**, **archived** (conceptual labels in mockups) | **Aid** reading—**avoid** false certainty inflation |

**Clarifications:** **Layers remain distinct** in planning sketches. **Visibility** (what appears “above the fold”) **must not** **collapse** authority boundaries into **one** undifferentiated slab.

---

### 3. Canon vs commentary presentation (ideas only)

- **Visually distinct bands** — typography/color **already** used on detail pages as **precedent**; planning may **extend** **language**, **not** ship code **here**.  
- **Authority indicators** — explicit **“Canon”** vs **“Commentary”** micro-labels in **wireframe** notes.  
- **Contextual annotations** — **sidebar** / **details** / **footnotes** patterns in **paper** sketches.  
- **Commentary boundaries** — framing lines that **stop** short of **doctrine** voice.  
- **Unresolved ambiguity markers** — **honest** “**open**” affordances per **CANON ANNOTATION**.  
- **Historical-note separation** — distinct from **current** binding text.  

**Clarifications:** **Explanation ≠ declaration.** **Annotation visibility ≠ canon authority** (**CANON EVIDENCE** stability epistemology applies by analogy).

---

### 4. Relationship & lineage presentation (ideas only)

- **Related sigils** — **typed** list: **doctrinal** vs **thematic** vs **speculative** (labels from **CANON ENTITY** taxonomy).  
- **Historical lineage** — **succession** strip or **footnote** chain **without** implying **equality**.  
- **Archived interpretations** — **collapsed** by default; **expand** reveals **disclaimed** text.  
- **Symbolic associations** — **low** visual **weight**; **pattern** not **proof**.  
- **Relationship confidence** — **badge** or **caption** per **CANON ENTITY** confidence model.  
- **Unresolved links** — explicit **“unresolved”** state **visible**.  

**Clarifications:** **Any** future **association visualization** must **preserve** **confidence** and **authority** distinctions—**no** “**all** edges **green**” **defaults**.

---

### 5. Traceability & governance visibility

- **Governance references** — compact **lock** citations (title + date), **not** full **lock** text inlined.  
- **Lock lineage** — **supersedes** / **narrows** notes per **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION**.  
- **Review context** — **PR** link, **reviewer** posture (**non-promotional**).  
- **Evidence references** — point to **artifact** without **pretending** full **dossier** is evidence table.  
- **Historical notes** — **dated** snippets.  
- **Rationale visibility** — **why** a reading **shifted** (**deprecatedReason** analog in prose).  

**Clarifications:** **Traceability supplements** understanding; **not** all governance detail **must** dominate **reader-first** readability (**GOVERNANCE CONSOLIDATION** navigability goal).

---

### 6. Stability & authority signaling (conceptual indicators)

| Signal (mockup-level) | Typical use | Pitfall to avoid |
| --------------------- | ----------- | ------------------ |
| **Provisional canon** | **Transparent** tier label | **Anxiety** inflation |
| **Stable canon** | **Quiet** confidence | **False** “**immutable forever**” |
| **Historical artifact** | **Archive** ribbon | **Confusing** with **current** law |
| **Archived / deprecated** | **Disclaimer** band | **Shame** tone vs **honest** context |
| **Commentary** | **Muted** chrome | **Mimicking** **doctrine** gold |
| **Speculative interpretation** | **Dashed** / **“maybe”** affordance | **Presenting** as **fact** |
| **Governance-confirmed relationship** | **Cited** edge type | **Implying** Zierota said **more** than **lock** text |

**Clarifications:** Signaling **aids** understanding **without** **certainty inflation**—no **badge** that **implies** proof **absent** **CANON EVIDENCE** path.

---

### 7. Observational pressure testing

Use the **specimen** narrative (and **live** **Top-Iron** page as **reference**) to **watch** for:

- **Readability** — scan path, fatigue, **wall of text**  
- **Annotation overload** — too many **parallel** voices  
- **Authority confusion** — readers **misread** commentary as canon  
- **Relationship clutter** — too many **edges** **without** typing  
- **Archive noise** — history **drowning** **present** contract  
- **Traceability usability** — stewards **cannot** find **why**  
- **Operational friction** — **edit**/**review** cost to keep layers honest  
- **Implementation pressure** — urge to **schema** everything **early**  

**Clarifications:** Observations **may inform** future governance or implementation **refinement**; **this prototype lock** **does not** **amend** constitutional text—changes go through **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** / **dedicated** locks.

---

### 8. Future implementation boundary

- **Future UI / data structures may evolve** — **separate** RFCs and **execution** locks.  
- **No implementation commitment** arises from **this** planning text alone.  
- **Prototype does not authorize schema migration** or **graph** stores.  
- **Tooling remains subordinate to governance** — **UI** cannot **declare** new **tier** rules.  
- **Mass-entry rollout** requires **explicit** program lock + **ingestion** discipline.  

---

### 9. Governance principles (explicit)

- **Readability matters.**  
- **Authority separation must remain visible.**  
- **Preserve constitutional boundaries** — planning **illustrates**, **does not** **rewrite**.  
- **Avoid semantic clutter.**  
- **Context should enrich rather than overwhelm.**  
- **Traceability should remain accessible** without **colonizing** the **doctrine** apex.  
- **Implementation does not redefine canon.**

- **No** entry modified **by this lock**; **no** **`sigils.json`** row added/changed **here**; **no** schema changed.

- **No** runtime, **CMS**, deploy, package, or automation changes **from this document**.
