## FULL ENTRY VISUAL MOCKUP — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **documentation / visual-conceptual planning only:** how **one** fully realized **specimen** codex entry **might** **visually** communicate canon **authority**, commentary, archive **history**, relationships, traceability, and **uncertainty** while preserving **constitutional** boundaries and **ceremonial** readability — **not** production UI rollout, **not** React/component or **CSS** implementation, **not** schema migration, **not** graph engine, **not** discoverability redesign, **not** canon authority change. **No** **`sigils.json`**, routes, CMS, deploy/package, or automation changes **from this lock**.

**Purpose:** **Pressure-test** constitutional **readability** **visually**; **observe** whether **authority** hierarchy stays **intuitively** legible; **evaluate** **atmospheric** coherence vs **governance** clarity; **surface** presentation **friction** before implementation; **validate** that constitutional **layers** remain **understandable** when **rendered** (in **paper**/**Figma**/**prose** sketch descriptions only).

**Relationship to other locks:** **Subordinate** to **FULL ENTRY PROTOTYPE — PHASE 1** (conceptual layer model — **this** lock adds **visual-treatment** vocabulary only). **Binds** to **CANON ANNOTATION**, **CANON ENTITY**, **CANON EVIDENCE**, **CONTENT** / **CANON TRANSITION** archive language, **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** traceability posture, and **AUTHORITATIVE POLICY ROOTS** (**doctrine-first**, **atmosphere protection**). **Live** reading reference: **TOP-IRON-ENDURANCE PHASE A IMPLEMENTATION** detail page.

**Current reality preserved:** **Cloudflare Pages** canonical; **PATH A** Pages CMS; **Decap**/**Identity** preserved; prior locks **unchanged** in **authority**; **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW** remains **active**; **no** graph tooling; **no** canon transitions **executed here**.

---

### 1. Visual prototype purpose

- **Test authority readability** — at-a-glance **doctrine** apex vs **peripheral** meta.  
- **Test canon / commentary separation** — **CANON ANNOTATION** in **layout** sketches only.  
- **Test annotation density** — side rails vs footnotes vs **collapsed** panels.  
- **Test relationship visibility** — **typed** lists / **strips** **without** graph edges in product.  
- **Test archive readability** — historical bands **distinct** from **current** binding surface.  
- **Test traceability accessibility** — compact **steward** strip vs **reader** body.  
- **Test emotional atmosphere vs governance clarity** — **ATMOSPHERE PROTECTION** vs **honest** labeling.  

**Clarifications:** The **visual prototype is observational**; it **does not redefine** governance. It **does not authorize** implementation rollout — **separate** execution locks and **RFC** gates apply.

---

### 2. Visual layer model (conceptual treatments)

| Layer | Conceptual visual treatment (sketch-level) | Authority / prominence note |
| ----- | -------------------------------------------- | ----------------------------- |
| **Canon body** | **Strongest** vertical band, **doctrine-first** gold/neutral hierarchy per existing detail grammar | **Apex** — **DOCTRINE-FIRST** root |
| **Commentary / annotation** | **Muted** rail, **lighter** weight, **labeled** “Commentary” / “Note” | **Subordinate** — **must not** **outshine** doctrine |
| **Historical / archive** | **Ribbon**, **dated** sub-band, or **collapsed** “Archive” disclosure | **Context** — **distinct** from **current** law |
| **Relationships** | **Typed** rows or **small** **captioned** clusters — **no** undifferentiated **mesh** | **Semantic** weight from **CANON ENTITY** — **visibility ≠ proof** |
| **Evidence / review** | **Compact** “Evidence / review” row — **not** a **wall** of dossier | **Process** clarity — **CANON EVIDENCE** |
| **Traceability** | **Footer** or **tertiary** column — **PR**, **lock** cite, **version** | **Accessible** but **secondary** to reading |
| **Governance references** | **Micro-citations** (lock title + date) — **no** inlined **full** lock text | **Meta** — **trust** without **noise** |
| **Implementation notes** | **Steward-only** sketch lane (if shown in internal boards) | **System** truth — **never** merged with **public** canon voice |
| **Authority / stability indicators** | **Quiet** tier labels, **dashed** speculative, **disclaimer** deprecated | **Orientation** — **no** **badge** that **implies** false **certainty** |

**Clarifications:** **Visual distinction must preserve authority distinction.** **Prominence** (size, contrast, motion) **must not** **silently inflate** authority — **visibility ≠ authority** (**CANON ANNOTATION** / **CANON ENTITY** analog).

---

### 3. Authority signaling philosophy (conceptual)

- **Stability badges** — **low-chrome** labels tied to **CONTENT** tier language **when** sketched; **avoid** “**immutable forever**” **tone**.  
- **Confidence indicators** — **caption-level** cues per **CANON EVIDENCE** / **CANON ENTITY** confidence model.  
- **Commentary labels** — explicit **microcopy** so **gloss** never **masquerades** as **doctrine**.  
- **Unresolved markers** — **open** / **disputed** affordances (**honest** ambiguity).  
- **Historical-state indicators** — **archive** / **deprecated** **ribbons** **visually** **separate** from **active** canon.  
- **Speculative relationship markers** — **dashed**, **“maybe”**, or **low-contrast** link style — **never** **solid** “confirmed” **chrome** without **governance-backed** declaration.  

**Clarifications:** Signaling **aids orientation** **without manufacturing false certainty.** **Visibility ≠ authority** — **loudest** element on the board **must remain** **doctrine** unless **explicitly** labeled otherwise.

---

### 4. Commentary & annotation presentation (ideas only)

- **Side annotations** — **narrow** column; **scroll-linked** only in **concept** notes (**not** shipped here).  
- **Collapsible contextual notes** — **default closed** for **dense** entries.  
- **Footnote-style references** — **small** numerals / **end-of-section** stacks.  
- **Layered commentary panels** — **tabs** or **accordions** labeled **non-doctrine**.  
- **Symbolic observation treatment** — **pattern** language **visually** **lighter** than **declared** geometry/doctrine rows.  
- **Unresolved ambiguity markers** — **icon + text** pair that **reads** as **“open”**, **not** as **error**.  

**Clarifications:** **Commentary supplements canon.** **Explanation ≠ declaration.** **Annotations must not visually overpower doctrine** — if a sketch **feels** “**wiki**” or **dashboard**, **reject** per **ATMOSPHERE PROTECTION**.

---

### 5. Relationship & lineage visualization (ideas only)

- **Doctrinal relationships** — **short** **typed** list, **highest** **trust** **weight** **within** relationship **zone** only.  
- **Thematic resonance** — **lower** contrast, **grouped** **apart** from **doctrinal** list.  
- **Speculative links** — **dashed** connectors or **“speculative”** tag — **never** **same** **solid** line as **declared** ties.  
- **Lineage / history** — **horizontal** **succession** strip or **vertical** **timeline** **footnote** — **no** **implied equality** of nodes.  
- **Archived interpretations** — **nested** under archive **disclosure**, **muted**.  
- **Unresolved relationships** — explicit **placeholder** state (**visible**, **non-shaming**).  

**Clarifications:** **Visualization must preserve confidence / authority distinctions.** **Relationship visibility must not imply truth inflation** — **no** “**all links green**” **defaults**; **no** **force-directed** **hero** graph in this phase.

---

### 6. Traceability & governance visibility

- **Lock lineage** — **one-line** **supersedes** / **narrows** note per **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** (sketch caption).  
- **Governance references** — **compact** citations; **link-out** to **CODEX** sections in **steward** materials.  
- **Evidence notes** — **pointer** row, **not** full **evidence table** **in** public **hero**.  
- **Review context** — **PR** / **reviewer** posture — **non-promotional** tone.  
- **Historical notes** — **dated**, **visually** **quarantined** from **binding** text.  
- **Rationale visibility** — **why** a reading **shifted** — **small** **prose**, **not** **banner** height.  

**Clarifications:** **Traceability should remain accessible** to stewards and **curious** readers. It **should not dominate** the **reading** experience. **Governance visibility should support trust, not overwhelm atmosphere.**

---

### 7. Atmospheric balance principles

- **Atmosphere + authority clarity simultaneously** — **ceremony** serves **meaning**, **labels** prevent **drift**.  
- **Readability over ornamental density** — **reject** **decorative** **noise** that **competes** with **hierarchy**.  
- **Constitutional hierarchy should feel intuitive** — **scan path** lands on **doctrine** first.  
- **Archive depth should enrich rather than bury** — **progressive disclosure** for **history**.  
- **Ambiguity may remain visible without causing confusion** — **clear** **“open”** semantics.  
- **Visual drama must not distort authority** — **no** **FX** or **contrast** tricks that **promote** commentary or **speculation**.  

---

### 8. Observational pressure testing

Use **specimen** sketches (and **live** **Top-Iron** detail as **tone** reference) to **watch** for:

- **Authority confusion** — commentary **read** as canon.  
- **Badge overreach** — **stability** chrome **implies** **unsupported** proof.  
- **Annotation overload** — **parallel** voices **fatigue** the eye.  
- **Archive noise** — **history** **drowns** **present** contract.  
- **Relationship clutter** — **too many** **untyped** adjacencies.  
- **Emotional readability** — **archive** **still** **feels** **inviting**, **not** **bureaucratic**.  
- **Navigation fatigue** — **too many** **disclosures** to **reach** doctrine.  
- **Constitutional legibility** — **layers** **map** to **mental model** of locks.  
- **Implementation pressure** — urge to **ship** sketches **without** **execution** lock.  

**Clarifications:** Observations **may inform** later **UI** refinement; **this mockup lock** **does not amend** governance — changes use **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** / **dedicated** locks.

---

### 9. Future implementation boundary

- **Future UI systems may evolve** from **insights** recorded here — **separate** **RFC** + **execution** planning.  
- **No implementation commitment** is created by **mockup** descriptions alone.  
- **No schema / graph authorization** implied — **data** shape remains **governed** elsewhere.  
- **Tooling remains subordinate to governance** — **CSS** or **components** cannot **declare** new **tier** rules.  
- **Rollout** of any **visual** system requires **explicit** program lock + **compatibility-first** checks (**COMPATIBILITY-FIRST EVOLUTION** root).  

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** UI **implemented** — **no** Astro/React/components, **no** CSS **authored** **under this lock**.  
- **No** schema changed; **no** relationships **implemented**; **no** graph tooling added.  
- **No** discoverability changes; **no** runtime behavior changed; **no** CMS, deploy, or package changes **from this document**.

## SPECIMEN ENTRY WIREFRAME — PHASE 1

**Status:** **LOCKED (2026-05-11)** — **documentation / structural wireframe planning only:** **low-fidelity** **layout-of-blocks** for **one** specimen codex entry to test whether **constitutional** hierarchy, authority **separation**, commentary **layering**, archive **visibility**, and traceability **remain understandable** **without** final **aesthetics**, styling, motion, or production UI systems — **not** production UI rollout, **not** React/**component** architecture lock, **not** CSS/**design**/**style** system, **not** graph engine, **not** schema migration, **not** discoverability redesign, **not** canon authority change. **No** **`sigils.json`**, routes, CMS, deploy/package, or runtime changes **from this lock**.

**Purpose:** **Pressure-test** constitutional readability as **pure structure**; **validate** information hierarchy **independent** of look-and-feel; **observe** whether authority stays **intuitive** in **neutral** wireframe form; **surface** layout **friction** before implementation; **ensure** governance **survives** **without** decorative reinforcement.

**Relationship to other locks:** **Subordinate** to **FULL ENTRY PROTOTYPE — PHASE 1** (conceptual layers). **Complements** **FULL ENTRY VISUAL MOCKUP — PHASE 1** — **this** lock owns **skeleton** (**order**, **containment**, **adjacency**); **visual** lock owns **chromatic**/**tonal** treatment — **neither** authorizes shipping UI **here**. **Binds** to **CANON ANNOTATION**, **CANON ENTITY**, **CANON EVIDENCE**, **CONTENT**/**CANON TRANSITION** archive posture, **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** traceability, **AUTHORITATIVE POLICY ROOTS** (**doctrine-first**, **sparse entry + density governance**). **Structural** reading reference: **TOP-IRON-ENDURANCE PHASE A IMPLEMENTATION** (existing detail **flow** as **precedent**, **not** a mandate to match every block).

**Current reality preserved:** **Cloudflare Pages** canonical; **PATH A** Pages CMS; **Decap**/**Identity** preserved; prior locks **unchanged** in **authority**; **SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW** remains **active**; **no** graph tooling; **no** canon transitions **executed here**.

---

### 1. Wireframe purpose

- **Test hierarchy without aesthetic assistance** — **grey boxes**, **numbered** **reading order**, **plain** prose labels only.  
- **Validate doctrine-first readability** — **canon** block **above** or **central** per **DOCTRINE-FIRST** root.  
- **Validate commentary separation** — **structurally** **non-interleaved** with **binding** paragraphs in sketches.  
- **Test archive containment** — history **does not** **swallow** active canon **in** block **topology**.  
- **Test relationship clarity** — **typed** **lists** / **regions**, **not** **hero** graph **zones**.  
- **Test traceability accessibility** — **footer** / **appendix** **lane** **reachable** **without** **front-loading**.  
- **Test constitutional legibility in low-fidelity form** — **steward** can **map** each **block** to a **governance** domain.  

**Clarifications:** The **wireframe is observational**; it **does not redefine** governance. It **does not authorize** implementation rollout — **execution** locks + **RFC** gates **still** required.

---

### 2. Structural layout model (low-fidelity blocks)

| Block / region (conceptual) | Structural role | Hierarchy / boundary note |
| --------------------------- | ----------------- | -------------------------- |
| **Canon body** | Primary **vertical** reading spine | **Apex** — **must** read as **first** contract |
| **Authority / stability indicators** | **Small** **meta** row **adjacent** to canon header **or** **inline** label strip — **not** a **second** doctrine column | **Orientation** — **must not** **expand** into **parallel** law |
| **Commentary / annotation** | **Secondary** column, **nested** subsection, or **below-the-fold** **panel** | **Subordinate** — **CANON ANNOTATION** |
| **Archive / history** | **Disclosed** region, **appendix** stack, or **separate** **“Archive”** **band** **after** active canon | **Contained** — **CONTENT** archive philosophy |
| **Relationships** | **Typed** **list** blocks (**doctrinal** / **thematic** / **speculative**) — **spatially** **grouped**, **not** **sprinkled** into doctrine | **CANON ENTITY** — **adjacency ≠ equality** |
| **Evidence / review** | **Single** **“Evidence / review”** **block** — **not** **interleaved** **per sentence** | **Process** weight — **CANON EVIDENCE** |
| **Governance references** | **Compact** **“Governed by”** **strip** | **Meta** — **no** full **lock** text **in** wireframe **body** |
| **Traceability** | **End** column: **PR**, **version**, **checkpoint** ids | **Reachable** — **secondary** to **reader** spine |
| **Implementation notes** | **Internal** board only — **optional** **lane** **outside** public **reading** path | **System** — **never** merged into **canon** **block** |

**Clarifications:** **Structure alone** should communicate **hierarchy** (order, size **as** “**large**/**small** **box**” **in** sketch sense only, **not** CSS). **Layout must not silently collapse** authority boundaries — **no** **single** undifferentiated **slab** mixing **doctrine** + **commentary** + **traceability** **without** **explicit** **region** labels.

---

### 3. Hierarchy-first principles

- **Doctrine remains primary even without styling** — if it **fails** in **grey boxes**, **ornament** will **not** **save** it.  
- **Commentary reads as secondary structurally** — **different** **region**, **lower** **in** **reading order**, or **explicit** **side** lane.  
- **Archive / history stays discoverable but contained** — **one** **clear** **entry** point; **default** **collapsed** in **dense** wireframes.  
- **Speculative material remains structurally subordinate** — **separate** list **or** **appendix** — **never** **inline** with **declared** canon **paragraphs**.  
- **Unresolved ambiguity remains distinguishable** — **labeled** **“open”** **sub-block**, **not** **hidden** in **footnotes-only** **unless** **footnote** **zone** is **explicitly** mapped.  
- **Traceability remains accessible without dominating** — **appendix** / **footer** **lane**, **not** **co-equal** column with doctrine.  

---

### 4. Commentary & archive containment (structural ideas)

- **Side lanes** — **narrow** **annotation** rail **with** **hard** **boundary** from **main** column.  
- **Nested sections** — **commentary** **child** **of** **canon** **parent** **only** **with** **explicit** **“Commentary”** **heading** in wireframe.  
- **Disclosure regions** — **archive** / **long** **historical** **chains** **behind** **single** **expand** affordance **in** sketch **legend**.  
- **Footnote zones** — **numbered** **anchors** from doctrine **point** to **end** **stack** — **must** **label** **non-doctrine**.  
- **Secondary panels** — **cards-as-boxes** **only** in **planning** boards — **not** **shipped** **components**.  
- **Layered reading paths** — **primary** path = **canon**; **secondary** = **meta**/**notes**/**relations**.  

**Clarifications:** **Commentary should enrich rather than interrupt** doctrine — **no** **mid-doctrine** **callout** **blocks** **without** **governance**-approved **exception** in **future** execution. **Archive material should not structurally bury** active canon — **active** **law** **finishes** **before** **deep** **history** **or** **disclosure** **opens** **below**.

---

### 5. Relationship & lineage structure (conceptual)

- **Doctrinal links** — **top** of **relationship** **zone**; **short** **list**; **explicit** **type** label **per** row.  
- **Thematic resonance** — **second** **sub-list** — **spatially** **below** **doctrinal**.  
- **Speculative relationships** — **third** **sub-list** or **dashed-border** **box** **in** sketch **legend** only (**not** CSS).  
- **Historical lineage** — **vertical** **timeline** **block** **or** **numbered** **succession** — **no** **implied** **node equality**.  
- **Archived interpretations** — **inside** **archive** **disclosure**, **not** **peer** to **current** **doctrine** **block**.  
- **Unresolved links** — **explicit** **placeholder** **rows** — **visible**, **typed** **“unresolved”**.  

**Clarifications:** **Structure must preserve confidence distinctions** (**CANON ENTITY**). **Relationship adjacency must not imply equality or proof** — **no** **undifferentiated** **“Related”** **bucket** **without** **internal** **typing**.

---

### 6. Traceability & governance accessibility (structural)

- **Lock lineage** — **one** **line** **in** **appendix**: **supersedes** / **narrows** (**GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION**).  
- **Evidence references** — **pointer** **list** — **not** **full** **dossier** **in** **primary** column.  
- **Governance notes** — **micro** **bullets** **linking** **out** to **CODEX** **sections** **(steward** **boards)**.  
- **Rationale visibility** — **small** **“Why”** **sub-block** **after** **archive** **or** **in** **traceability** **lane**.  
- **Review context** — **PR** / **reviewer** **row** **in** **traceability** **only**.  
- **Historical continuity** — **dated** **sub-blocks** **within** **archive** **region**.  

**Clarifications:** **Traceability should remain reachable** in **one** **deliberate** **scroll** **decision** — **not** **orphaned** **tabs** **without** **map**. **Governance metadata should not overwhelm** the **primary** reading **flow** — **no** **co-equal** **three-column** **law**/**governance**/**relations** **unless** **explicitly** **labeled** **experimental**.

---

### 7. Atmospheric neutrality test

- **Wireframe intentionally minimizes aesthetic reinforcement** — **no** **brand** **color** **commitments**, **no** **motion** **storyboards** **as** **authority** **proof** **in** this **phase**.  
- **Constitutional hierarchy should survive in neutral presentation** — **if** hierarchy **needs** **gold** **chrome** to **read**, **restructure** **first**.  
- **Aesthetics may later enrich structure but not rescue weak hierarchy** — **FULL ENTRY VISUAL MOCKUP** **layers** **on** **top** **only** **after** **skeleton** **holds**.  
- **Clarity should exist before ornamentation** — **SPARSE ENTRY** / **ATMOSPHERE PROTECTION** **compatible**: **quiet** **structure**, **not** **empty** **confusion**.  

---

### 8. Observational pressure testing

Use **specimen** **grey-box** flows (and **Top-Iron** detail **reading order** as **sanity** **check**) to **watch** for:

- **Hierarchy confusion** — **eye** **lands** **wrong** **first**.  
- **Commentary interruption** — **gloss** **breaks** **doctrine** **mid-thought**.  
- **Archive overload** — **history** **before** **contract**.  
- **Relationship clutter** — **one** **mega-list** **without** **types**.  
- **Traceability fatigue** — **steward** **cannot** **find** **locks** **without** **hunt**.  
- **Reading fragmentation** — **too many** **parallel** **columns**.  
- **Governance noise** — **meta** **competes** with **lore**.  
- **Implementation pressure toward premature styling** — **urge** to **open** **Figma** **tokens** **before** **locking** **blocks**.  

**Clarifications:** Observations **may inform** later **refinement**; **this wireframe lock** **does not amend** governance — **GOVERNANCE EVOLUTION** / **dedicated** locks **for** **text** **changes**.

---

### 9. Future implementation boundary

- **Future UI systems may evolve** from **wireframe** **insights** — **separate** **RFC** + **execution** planning.  
- **No implementation commitment** from **block** **diagrams** **or** **prose** **ordering** **alone**.  
- **No schema / graph authorization** implied — **edges** **exist** **only** **on** **paper** **here**.  
- **Styling remains subordinate to constitutional readability** — **CSS** **cannot** **reorder** **authority** **without** **lock**.  
- **Rollout** requires **explicit** program lock + **compatibility-first** checks (**COMPATIBILITY-FIRST EVOLUTION** root).  

---

### 10. No-behavior-change statement

- **No** UI **implemented** — **no** Astro/React/**components**, **no** routes changed **by** this **document**.  
- **No** CSS or **design**/**style** **system** created; **no** **visual** **design** **lock** **established** **here**.

## DISPLAY METADATA UI RFC

**Status:** documentation / planning only — **no** `sigils.json`, schema, CMS, or component edits until a controlled implementation phase.

### 1. Purpose

Plan **safe, restrained** rendering of optional display metadata — **`title`**, **`meaning`**, **`layer`** — so the public codex can surface editorial enrichments **without** upsetting the **ceremonial archive** tone or **doctrine-first** hierarchy.

### 2. Candidate UI locations (evaluation)

| Surface | Role | Risk / note |
| ------- | ---- | ----------- |
| **`/showcase`** cards | Already uses adapter **`title`** on grid | Adding **`meaning`**/**`layer`** risks busy curated tiles |
| **`/sigils`** browse cards | Dense grid; primary job is scan + enter detail | **High** clutter risk if **`meaning`**/**`layer`** appear here early |
| **`/sigils/[slug]`** detail | Full doctrine + Classification | **Low** layout risk; strongest context for short summary + archive line |
| **Classification block** | Structured catalogue rows | Mixing optional display fields with **geometry**/**usage** may blur semantics — prefer **separate** subtle block unless taxonomy aligns |
| **Hero / featured** (showcase) | Single spotlight | Could mirror detail treatment later; not required for first rollout |

### 3. Recommended first UI surface

**`sigils/[slug]` detail page only** — first implementation surface.

**Reasons:**

- **Lowest public layout risk** — single-column reading flow already established.
- **Strongest doctrine context** — **`meaning`** reads as a **short lead** into full **`doctrine`**, not marketing copy.
- **Avoids busy browse** — **`SigilCard`** stays lean until a later RFC proves density is acceptable.
- **Canon-aligned** — metadata supports reading, not promotion.

### 4. Display rules

| Field | Rule |
| ----- | ---- |
| **`title`** | Optional **display** heading override **only where product adopts adapter for `<h1>`**; must not fight **`name`** for routing/SEO without an explicit decision; if shown, same restrained typography as current title. |
| **`meaning`** | Render **only if** present in data — short **doctrine summary** line (neutral tone), placed **above or immediately before** full Doctrine block — **never** duplicated as fake subtitle when absent. |
| **`layer`** | Render **only if** present — **subtle archive metadata** (e.g. small label row or muted line), **no** badge stacks — **never** placeholders (**“Unknown layer”**, etc.). |
| **Missing fields** | **No** fabricated UI; **no** fallbacks that invent labels — omit sections entirely. |

### 5. Atmosphere constraints

Maintain:

- **Restrained ceremonial archive** — no flash, no promotional stripes.
- **Doctrine-first** — full **`doctrine`** remains the authoritative gold block; **`meaning`** is auxiliary when present.
- **Symbolic codex tone** — typography/spacing consistent with existing Classification / Doctrine sections.
- **No** marketing-style cards, **no** noisy badges, **no** over-labeling every optional key.

### 6. Rollout plan (staged)

| Stage | Scope |
| ----- | ----- |
| **A** | **Detail page** — optional compact **Display metadata** subsection (or lead-in lines): **`meaning`**, **`layer`** when present; optional **`title`** vs **`name`** policy decided before coding. |
| **B** | **`SigilCard`** — only if Stage A proves stable and editorial wants browse parity (still minimal). |
| **C** | **`/showcase`** — refine only **after** A (and B only if needed); avoid duplicating long metadata on hero/grid. |

### 7. Validation requirements (future implementation)

Implementation gate:

- Entries **without** optional fields render **identically** to today (no empty boxes).
- **IAH-VEA** shows **`meaning`** / **`layer`** correctly when keys present.
- No layout regression at **`max-w-2xl`**; mobile spacing unchanged in spirit.
- **Search / discoverability / Fuse / routes** unchanged.
- **`npm run build`** + **`npx astro check`** PASS.

### 8. Next recommended implementation phase

**DETAIL PAGE DISPLAY METADATA — CONTROLLED IMPLEMENTATION**

Scope: **`src/pages/sigils/[slug].astro`** (+ minimal shared styling if needed); **`toSigilDisplayItem(sigil)`** or conditional reads of **`sigil.meaning`** / **`sigil.layer`** / optional **`title`** **only** per rules above — **after** this RFC is accepted.

---

## DETAIL PAGE DISPLAY METADATA — CONTROLLED IMPLEMENTATION

**Status:** **Locked** — optional display metadata on **`/sigils/[slug]`** only (see post-validation notes below).

**Non-authoritative declaration:** Optional **`title`**, **`meaning`**, and **`layer`** are **editorial / archival assists** for reading. They **do not** supersede **`name`**, **`doctrine`**, Classification, routing, discoverability, or canon source text.

### Implementation scope

- **Files:** **`src/pages/sigils/[slug].astro`** exclusively for this phase (no **`SigilCard`**, no **`showcase`**, no shared component refactor unless unavoidable).
- **Adapter:** Call **`toSigilDisplayItem(sigil)`** on the detail route; render adapter-backed strings **only** where the underlying optional JSON field is **present** (see omission behavior — **`meaning`** must **not** use adapter fallback derived from doctrine when the optional key is absent).

### Detail-page-only rule

Browse (**`/sigils`**) and showcase surfaces stay unchanged; optional metadata appears **only** on the sigil detail template.

### Metadata hierarchy

1. **`name`** remains the stable primary heading (**`<h1>`**) and canonical identity on the page.
2. Optional **`title`** (when present and distinct from **`name`**) may appear as a **single restrained line** — archival gloss, not a replacement headline.
3. **`meaning`** (when present): one short **muted** line **before** the Doctrine section — doctrine-adjacent lead, not marketing subtitle.
4. **`layer`** (when present): **subtle** archive metadata (low dominance), typically below **`meaning`** when both exist.
5. Full **`doctrine`** block remains the authoritative reading body (**doctrine-first**).

### Omission behavior

- Missing optional fields produce **no** DOM for that field — **no** placeholders, **no** “Unknown …”, **no** adapter-invented **`meaning`** from doctrine unless **`meaning`** exists in JSON.
- Sigils without optional metadata match prior layout (no empty regions).

### Rollback simplicity

Revert or strip the optional markup block(s) in **`[slug].astro`** — **no** schema, CMS, JSON, or route changes required for rollback.

### Atmosphere constraints

- Ceremonial archive tone; restrained spacing; **no** badge stacks, **no** metadata cards/panels, **no** dashboard or spec-sheet framing.
- Annotation sits **at the edge** of doctrine — thin typography, muted neutrals / amber-adjacent restraint consistent with existing sections.

### Validation requirements

- **`npm run build`** and **`npx astro check`** PASS.
- **`iah-vea`** (pilot): optional lines render correctly; other public sigils unchanged visually except intentional pilot lines.
- No discoverability, Fuse, taxonomy, or routing changes.

### Locked implementation notes (post-validation)

**Rendering locations (`src/pages/sigils/[slug].astro`):**

| Optional field | Placement | Source |
| -------------- | --------- | ------ |
| **`title`** | One line **below** **`<h1>`** (`sigil.name`), only when **`title`** is present **and** trim‑distinct from **`name`** | **`display.title`** (`toSigilDisplayItem`) |
| **`meaning`** | Muted paragraph **after** **`SigilMeta`** / classification chips strip, **before** Doctrine heading | **`display.meaning`** — rendered **only** when **`sigil.meaning`** is non-empty (adapter doctrine extraction **not** shown without JSON key) |
| **`layer`** | Uppercase micro-label line below **`meaning`** when both exist; alone same block | **`display.layer`** — only when **`sigil.layer`** is non-empty |

**Document title:** **`Layout`** `title` remains **`${sigil.name} · Empyrria Sigil Codex`** (stable SEO/route identity string).

**Omission:** Absent keys → no markup for that field; no placeholders.

**Styling:** Restrained neutrals — ceremonial **`title`** `text-sm` muted; **`meaning`** doctrine-adjacent body-muted; **`layer`** `text-[0.65rem]` uppercase tracking — **no** panels, badges, or dashboard framing.

**Validation results:** **`npm run build`** — PASS (**`validate:content`** included); **`npx astro check`** — PASS (**2026-05-09**).

**Rollback:** Remove optional blocks in **`[slug].astro`** (adapter import + gates); no data/schema/CMS edits.

**Next recommended phase:** RFC Stage **B** — optional **`SigilCard`** lines **only if** editorial need; **or** CMS widgets for optional fields; **or** second enrichment pilot sigil — **not** required for MVP stability.

- **Approved canon source ≠ draft preservation:** Sections under **`## DRAFT — NOT APPROVED (DO NOT INGEST)`** in **`canon/EMPYRRIA_SIGIL_CODEX_SOURCE.md`** are continuity records only—they are **not** approved canon and **must not** populate `sigils.json` until promoted to **`## SIGIL ENTRIES`** with **`Status: Approved`**.
- **`canon/EMPYRRIA_SIGIL_CODEX_SOURCE.md`** (approved blocks only—or equivalently approved source) **before** `src/data/sigils.json`.

## Library MVP — requirements

- **Browse** sigils as cards on `/sigils`.
- **Search** across name, doctrine, and facets (client-side Fuse.js on `/sigils`; `underlay` is not in the Fuse key list today — add it if product wants full-text search there).
- **Filter** by facet (category).
- **Sort** (original JSON order, A–Z, Z–A by name).
- **Detail view** at `/sigils/[slug]`: doctrine (gold tone), optional **Classification** block (neutral label/value rows for `geometry`, `usage`, `color`, `terms`, `category` when present in JSON), underlay (cyan tone), optional SVG image, facets.
- **Data:** single JSON pack (`src/data/sigils.json`) validated at build time (`npm run build` runs `validate:content`).
- **Legacy MVP checklist** also listed an **About** page — there is still **no** `/about` route (see gaps below).

---

## Current data structure

Authoritative constraints: `src/data/sigils.schema.json`. Loader/helpers: `src/lib/sigils.ts`.

Root document:

| Field | Role |
| ----- | ---- |
| `$schema` | JSON Schema reference |
| `version` | Data pack version (shown on home) |
| `sigils` | Array of sigil records |

Per sigil (keys used in repo):

| Field | Role |
| ----- | ---- |
| `slug` | Stable URL segment (`/sigils/[slug]`) |
| `name` | Display title |
| `title` | Optional display override (adapter; falls back to `name`) |
| `doctrine` | Doctrine text |
| `meaning` | Optional short meaning line (adapter; falls back to heuristic from `doctrine`) |
| `layer` | Optional archive / system layer label |
| `underlay` | System / context text |
| `category` | Optional primary canonical classification label |
| `facets` | String array — browse/filter taxonomy tags (see **Category vs facets** below) |
| `image` | Optional public path (SVG preferred); see **Sigil images** below |
| `canonStatus` | Optional when present |
| `geometry`, `usage`, `color` | Optional strings; shown on detail **Classification** when non-empty |
| `terms` | Optional string array; shown as compact chips when non-empty |

**Category vs facets:** `category` is the **primary canonical classification** label for an entry. `facets` drive **browse/filter** on `/sigils`; keep them **taxonomy-oriented** (role in the system, e.g. State Sigil) and avoid drift into mood-only or loose aesthetic tags unless canon defines them. Current data often duplicates the same string in both fields for simplicity — no migration required; future multi-facet entries should still treat `facets` as tags, not vibes.

CMS/editor contract: **Pages CMS** — **`.pages.yml`** (repo root; governance-hardened **Zierota** profile; branch-aware). **Decap** — `public/admin/config.yml` and archived **STEP 12 — CMS FIELD MODEL** in `EMPYRRIA_PHILOSOPHY_ARCHIVE.md` (**legacy / rollback**).

### Sigil images (optional assets)

- **`image` is optional** — browse cards and detail pages omit the visual plate when no path is set; layout stays valid with text-only entries.
- **Paths:** commit files under `public/media/sigils/`; JSON value like `/media/sigils/<file>.svg` (build validator enforces path prefix and file presence when set).
- **UI:** Square neutral **plates** (subtle border, dark fill, `object-contain`) on cards and detail so silhouettes stay readable at small sizes; not hero imagery, no glow. **Alt text:** `{name} sigil` when an image is shown.
- **First canonical assets:** Soulflame, Top-Clear-Mind, and Zenga Zellia ship with curated SVG line art (`soulflame.svg`, `top-clear-mind.svg`, `zenga-zellia.svg`); pipeline and layout validated with live files; silhouettes kept simple for card-scale readability.

## IAH-VEA — stabilization micro-fix — locked

**Issues addressed:** broken plate image; **`/sigils/iah-vea`** reported **404**.

**Root causes:**

1. **SVG:** **`public/media/sigils/iah-vea.svg`** contained an invalid UTF-8 / replacement character in the HTML comment, which can cause strict XML/SVG parsers to reject the file → broken `<img>` in cards/detail.
2. **Route:** **`slug`**: **`iah-vea`** and **`getPubliclyDiscoverableSigils()`** were already correct; static build emits **`dist/sigils/iah-vea/index.html`**. **`404`** typically indicates **`astro dev`** started before **`sigils.json`** included the row (**restart dev**) or viewing an old **`dist`** / deployment without rebuilding.

**Changes:** **`iah-vea.svg`** — ASCII-only comment line; **same paths, geometry, colors**.

**Validation:** `npm run build`; `npx astro check` — **PASS** (recorded at lock).

**no** authority or **meaning** changes). **Current governance mode:** **`SELECTIVE MATURATION PAUSE + OBSERVATIONAL STABILITY WINDOW`** and **`STEWARDSHIP MODE TRANSITION RECORD`** — **locked** (observation-first, non-expansion stewardship posture).

## MASTER DOCUMENT CLEANUP PASS

**Status:** **LOCKED** — structure + cleanup pass complete (**documentation-only**; no schema/CMS/UI/data semantics changes).

### Major reorganizations

- Added **CANONICAL DOCUMENT STRUCTURE — STABLE** to establish the seven-band long-term organization model.
- Added a normalized **Status Vocabulary** and **Consolidation Rule** to reduce drift and repeated policy wording.
- Normalized operational section headings for scanability:
  - **OPERATIONAL STATE — CURRENT LIVE CODEX**
  - **OPERATIONAL STATE — ACTIVE DEVELOPMENT PHASE**
  - **OPERATIONAL STATE — CURRENT NEXT STEP**

### Normalization decisions

- Standardized top-level status language around **LOCKED / DOCUMENTED / ACTIVE / DEFERRED / STABLE**.
- Declared policy consolidation behavior: reuse authoritative governance sections instead of copying protection lists into every phase block.
- Kept existing RFC names and lock records intact; this pass normalizes structure/navigation, not historical labels.

### Preserved historical sections

- All major RFC outcomes, lock chronology, and implementation history remain preserved.
- Selective enrichment execution records (IAH-VEA, Soulflame, Top-Clear-Mind) remain unchanged in substance.
- Phase A system lineage (spec, wireframe, implementation plan, implementation, atmosphere pass, consistency audit) remains intact.

### Redundancy cleanup

- Reduced governance repetition pressure by introducing an explicit consolidation rule.
- Eliminated stale operational contradiction in live-state summary:
  - Updated public sigil count to **six**
  - Added **Top-Iron-Endurance** to live SVG assets
- Updated active-phase wording to reflect current locked state set.

### Navigation improvements

- Document now has a stable up-front structure map for future growth.
- Operational-state headings are grouped and clearly named for quick scans.
- Cleanup pass itself is documented as a lockable governance event for future audits.

### Current canonical structure

1. **PROJECT IDENTITY**
2. **GOVERNANCE LAYER**
3. **CORE ARCHITECTURE**
4. **IMPLEMENTATION LAYER**
5. **EDITORIAL EXECUTIONS**
6. **FUTURE / DEFERRED SYSTEMS**
7. **OPERATIONAL STATE**

### Unresolved areas

- Legacy section order remains historically layered rather than physically re-chunked into strict contiguous bands to preserve chronological audit trails.
- If desired later, a pure physical reorder can be done as a separate **documentation-only migration pass** with line-by-line cross-reference verification.

## AUTHORITATIVE POLICY ROOTS CONSOLIDATION PASS

**Status:** **LOCKED** — governance consolidation layer applied (**documentation-only**; no schema/CMS/UI/data/canon-meaning changes).

### Consolidated policy roots

- Added **AUTHORITATIVE POLICY ROOTS — STABLE** with six canonical roots:
  1. **DOCTRINE-FIRST GOVERNANCE — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**
  2. **ATMOSPHERE PROTECTION — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**
  3. **SPARSE ENTRY + DENSITY GOVERNANCE — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**
  4. **PROSE-PRESERVATION GOVERNANCE — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**
  5. **COMPATIBILITY-FIRST EVOLUTION — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**
  6. **SELECTIVE ENRICHMENT GOVERNANCE — AUTHORITATIVE ROOT**

### Normalized references

- Selective-enrichment execution charters now cite roots directly for recurring doctrine/atmosphere constraints instead of repeating full protection lists.
- Consolidation rule updated to point future phases toward root citations by default.

### Preserved chronology and lineage

- Historical RFC content, lock chronology, and execution sequence remain intact.
- No historical section was removed; consolidation is additive and referential.

### Reduced duplication

- Repeated doctrine-first and atmosphere boilerplate in pass charters replaced with root references while preserving pass-specific tonal qualifiers.
- Core protections remain unchanged in meaning; only citation style and duplication burden were normalized.

### Navigation improvements

- Policy discoverability improved through a single stable root cluster near the top of the document.
- Each root now includes intent + “Referenced by” guidance for faster audit and maintenance.

### Unresolved future cleanup considerations

- Additional legacy sections still contain repeated anti-wiki / anti-schema language for historical context; further compression should be done gradually to avoid over-sterilizing chronology.
- A later optional pass can add lightweight cross-links from older RFC subsections directly to root IDs for tighter navigability.

| Command | Purpose |
| ------- | ------- |
| `npm run build` | Runs `validate:content` then `astro build` — **required** |
| `npx astro check` | Astro + TypeScript check |
| `npm run check:links` | Internal link scan (manual workflow today) |

Manual smoke (hosted or `npm run dev`):

- `/`, `/sigils`, `/sigils/iah-vea`, **`/sigils/top-iron-endurance`** (Phase **A** prototype row), other live slugs, `/codex`, `/codex/what-is-a-sigil`, `/codex/system-architecture`, `/showcase`
- Browse: search, filter, sort behave as expected
- `/admin` loads Decap shell if relevant to the change
